A na n+da syA da @# /
bod kyi lo rgyus r+sha nA ma b+ho Ta syA k+ti kun dga'i me long zhes bi ha ra ti sma / /
bya ba bzhugs so /

sdeb sbyor mnyam pa'i br-it+ta las yi ge bcu gnyis pa skye 'gro la spyir grangs bzhi stong go drug mchis pa las bye brag 'dir stong dang brgya don gcig pa me tog 'phreng can zhes bya ba'i prastA ras mdzes par spras pa'o /
@# / /
tse di taiH su nr-i taM d+ha rma yo rla k+Sha aM @# / /
bden gtam chos kyi 'od snang 'bum bkye bas / /
shu rka raH br-i t+ta mi srA mr-i ShaH dA ra NaH / /
brdzun gtam smag rum stug po 'joms mdzad pa / /
bai na yaH pra ShTHa mau niH a di rbai na yaH rnam 'dren thub pa mchog sogs rnam 'dren rnams / /
pU dza sa rba tra kAM U D+ha A sa rba tra / /
gtan bde ma reg bar du gtan du mchod / /
bden gtam chos kyi 'od snang 'bum bkye bas / /
rdzun gtam smag rum stug po 'joms mdzad pa / /
rnam 'dren thub pa mchog sogs rnam 'dren rnams / /
gtan bde ma reg bar du gtan du mchod / /
mkhyen pa'i mkha' la thos pa'i sprin bsags nas / /
mdo rgyud legs bshad dbyangs kyi g.yu 'brug ldir / /
lo rgyus smra ba'i ljags dmar glog zhags che / /
rkyong mdzad mkhas dbang mtha' dag phyag gi yul / /
bsil ldan khams su chags pa'i mun pa'i dgra / /
chos srid nyi zla zung gi 'od spro ba / /
rgyal blon lo paN mkhas grub klu dbang 'bum / /
gangs ljongs mtsho chen rgyas pa'i dpyid du shar / /
de yi byung ba gzugs brnyan gzigs mo 'bum / /
yongs su shar ba'i kun dga'i me long zhig /
lo rgyus rig pa smra ba'i mkhas gral du / /
snyeg 'dod gzhon nu dga' ba'i skyes su 'bul / /
ji skad du /
bka' gdams glegs bam las /
shar rdo rje gdan gyi byang phyogs na / /
gnas pur rgyal bod ces bya ba yod / /
ri mthon po gnam gyi ka ba yod / /
mtsho dma' mo g.yu yi maN Dal yod / /
gangs dkar bo shel gyi mchod rten yod / /
spang ser bo gser gyi lhun po yod / /
dri zhim po sman gyi bdug spos yod / /
ston bkra ba gser gyi me tog yod / /
dbyar bkra ba g.yu yi me tog yod / /
kye gangs ri'i mgon po spyan ras gzigs / /
gnas de na khyod kyi zhing khams yod / /
zhing de na khyod kyi gdul bya yod / /
ces bsngags pa'i pur rgyal bod ces bya ba'i zhing khams kyi lo rgyus mdor bsdus te brjod par bya'o / /
le'u dang bo /
bod spyi'i lo rgyus bshad pa /
dang bo /
snod bcud chags tshul /
de yang bod yul 'di ni sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa sangs rgyas pa'i gnas rgya gar rdo rje gdan gyi byang phyogs su yod la /
ljongs 'di'i phyi snod kyi 'jig rten dang /
nang bcud kyi sems can gnyis ka gna' ches snga mo zhig nas chags shing /
ming la'ang 'dod rgyal gyi ming bod ces pa ches snga mo zhig nas 'bod pa yin te /
deb ther dmar bo gsar ma las /
lung rnam 'byed dang /
dpal dus kyi 'khor lo sogs su bod ces mang du byung bas /
bdag cag gi ston pa shAkya thub pa 'jig rten du byon pa'i dus las yul dang mi gnyis ka ches snga bar chags pa zhig snang /
zhes gsungs pa don la gnas so / /
tshul 'di la ni bod kyi lo rgyus smra ba'i mkhas dbang phal mo che mgrin gcig yin te /
nel ba paN Di ta /
stag tshang lo tsA ba /
bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa /
'gos lo gzhon nu dpal sogs kyis /
bod kyi yul 'di rgya gar dang 'dra bar yul dang mi la sogs pa gnas pa'i bskal pa nas byung ba byas na yang /
lung dang rigs pas gnod pa med ces gsungs so / /
yul 'dir ri lung chags nas mi'i 'gro ba ma chags pa'i sngon du /
ri lung thams cad chus gang nas yod par bshad /
de rjes chu 'khyil sa'i yol go rnams kyi kha shor te chu rnams rgya mtshor bzhur ba'i shul du rim gyis rtsi shing nags tshal rgyas /
de nas rim gyis srog chags dag grub pa yin te /
stod mnga' ris kyi cha ni glang bo che dang ri dwags kyi yul /
bar dbus gtsang gi cha ni ri dwags dang spre'u'i yul /
smad mdo khams kyi cha ni spre'u dang brag srin gyi yul du gyur to / /
de yang stod g.ya' ri dang brag ri /
bar brag dang spang ljongs /
smad rtsi shing dang nags tshal gyi yul du gyur nas lo ches mang bar mi'i 'gro ba med la /
yang stod mnga' ris skor gsum gyi sa 'di gangs dang g.ya'i ra ba yod pas rdzing dang 'dra bar bshad /
bar dbus gtsang ru bzhi yod sa 'di brag dang chu 'thab sa yur ba dang 'dra bar bshad /
smad mdo khams sgang drug gi sa 'di nags dang na'i ljongs zhing dang 'dra bar bshad do / /
ljongs 'dir mi'i 'gro ba chags tshul ni /
gna' ches snga mor yul dbus gtsang gi phyogs spra dang spre'us gang ba'i dus shig tu lho kha sne gdong gi phyogs kyi brag mgon po'i ri la gnas pa'i spre'u byang chub sems dpa' dang brag srin mo 'dus pa las sprel phrug mang du 'phel ba las rim gyis mir gyur pa'i rgyud las byung zhing /
sprel phrug rnams nags tshal du gnas te shing thog gi 'tsho ba byas nas bsdad pas mang du 'phel /
bar skabs shig nas gzhung gi chu rnams bzhur ba'i shul du spang gzhongs rgya chen po byung /

thang de'i sa zhing ni spre'u rnams kyis sa bon btab ste 'bru rigs 'khrungs skabs /
phan tshun zo dang zhes pa'i mi'i skad smra shes par gyur pas /

zhing la snga ba zo dang zhing zhes grags pa dang /

khog grim pa /
ma rigs rnams gdong dmar sdig las la rngam zhing ro gyong ba /

rus chen bzhi las gyes pa'i khams ni /

dper na /
sga la da dga' dang /
sa sga gnyis ka 'byung ba dang /
sbra la da dbra dang sa sbra gnyis ka 'byung ba dang /

gling ge sar gyi sgrung du smug po gdong gi mi rgyud ces bris pa mang la /
mi'u gdung drug gi rus mdzod nang du smug po ldong gi rgyud pa zhes bris pa lta bu'o / /

de ltar byas tshe /
rus chen bzhi ni /
sga 'bru sbra gdong bzhi'am /
sga 'bru sbra ldong bzhi zhes 'dren pa yin snang /
mdo khams stod smad du sga 'bru'i rigs mang la /
sbra rigs kyang rgyal mo tsha ba rong gi mi lta bu dang /
ldong rigs kyang gling ge sar gyi mi rgyud da lta yod pa dang mdo stod smad kun tu yod de /
rus mdzod las /
'gag dog mo gsum po sbra yis bzung / /
sbra dpa' rtsal che ba de don yin / /
zhes dang /
ri mthon po gsum po gdong gis bzung / /
gdong zhwa mgo mtho ba de don yin / /
zhes zer ba lta bu yin la /
mdo khams kyi lo rgyus skabs su 'bri'o / /
bod kyi mi'i rigs kyi byung tshul sogs ni /
srong btsan sgam po yan du yi ger bkod pa med la /
srong btsan sgam pos sngon gyi bshad rgyun dag pa rnams yi ger bkod de chud mi za ba'i phyir gter du sbas pa bka' chems bka' khol ma dang /
ma Ni bka' 'bum sogs ji snyed cig yod pa rnams /
yi ge rgyun 'byams dang drung yig sogs kyis bris bshus sna tshogs kyi dbang gis 'dra min 'ga' re mchis mod /
don gyi dgongs pa'i khog gcig yin stabs /
spre'u dang brag srin mo lhan cig tu 'dus pa'i phru gu gdong dmar sha zan gyi rigs su bshad pa ni /
yab mes dag gi bshad rgyun yang dag pa red do / /
des na spre'u mir gyur te mi'i 'gro ba chags pa ni snga la /
lha las phul byung gi bstod pa'i 'grel ba shes rab go chas mdzad pa las gsungs pa ltar /
rtsod ldan thog ma'i skabs /
skyabs seng bu lnga'i dmag 'khrug byung nas /
g.yul bkyes pa'i tshe ru pa ti bya ba'i rgyal bo g.yul las pham nas dpung tshogs gcig dang bcas bud med kyi cha lugs su byas te bros nas /
ri kha ba can gyi khrod du zhugs te gnas pa'i rigs la bod ces grags pa yin gsungs pa ltar /
gnyug mar gnas pa'i sprel rigs kyi mi'i steng du de dag las 'phel ba'i rigs kyang yod de /
rdog rabs gsal ba'i me long las /
" bod kyi gtam rgyud dag las spre'u dang brag srin mo las 'phel ba dag ni zur du shes la /
rdog 'di rgya gar nas chad pa yin te /
de yang rtsod dus steng nas ring zhig lon pa na /
rgya gar du rgyal bo yul 'khor skyong gi sras g.yul ngor brtan pa /
zhes sam /
dgra ngan zhes kyang bya ba dpung tshogs bcu gnyis sam /
lha las phul byung gi bstod pa'i 'grel bar dpung tshogs bco brgyad zer ba /
rgyal bo skyabs seng gi bu lnga /
tsha bo dang drug khyab 'jug dang bdun gyis bcom nas /
dgra ngan gum pa'i tshe dgra ngan gyi chab srid nyams /
skyabs seng gi bu mnga' ris su yod pa la /
rgyal bo ru pa ti zhes bya ba dang /
blon po rdog gi mgo byas /
mi stong phrag gcig bud med kyi chas su zhugs nas /
ri gangs can gyi gseb tu bros pa las 'phel lo / /
rdog gi rgyud pa 'di mdo khams shar tsong kha'i yul dang nye ba na /
rdog gi sde che bar chags so / /
" zhes gsungs pa ltar /
skyabs seng gi phyis kyi bu rgyud cig yin par snang /
mi rgyud de ni phyis su byung bar gsal la /
rdog gi mi rgyud 'di ni mdo smad kyi rnga ba dang dmu dge sogs su'ang yod /
'on kyang rdog gi yi ge dbu can 'bri tshe da dang nga gnyis nor nas /
rdog nyi ma seng ges mdzad pa'i gze ma ra mgo la rngog gi gze ma ra mgo dang /
rdog ar ya de ba la rngog ar ya de ba zhes bris pa dang /
'don pa mang la de bzhin du dbu can gyi nga dang da nor ba mang ste /
dper na /
brda rnying gi shi dge /
'dad btang zhes pa yi ge ma dag pa'i rjes su 'brangs nas /
deng sang 'dang btang zhes 'bri mkhan yod pa lta bu'o / /
der ma zad de las gzhan pa'i mi rigs las chad pa'i rigs kyang yod nges so / /
de ltar sprel rgyud las byung ba'i mi dag thog mar shing thog dang rgod skyes 'bru rigs dang rngon byed pa sogs kyis 'tsho zhing rim gyis zhing 'brog gi las kyang dar nas sde shog gi lam lugs sogs dar zhing /
phyi nas 'ongs pa'i chos lugs 'ga' re'ang byung ba 'dra zhing dar khyab ma byung bar mngon /
'on kyang /
lha mchod 'dre mchod byed mkhan dag la ni bon zhes 'bod par snang ste /
dper na /
deng dus su'ang gto chog mdos chog byed pa la bon byed ces gzhung du mar gsungs 'dug pa bzhin no / /
gnyis pa /
bod spyi la dbang ba'i rgyal bo gnya' khri btsan po /
bod spyi la dbang ba'i rgyal bo'i thog ma ni gnya' khri btsan po yin te /
rgyal bo la snga ba gnya' khri btsan po zhes grags so / /
rgyal bo 'di spyi lo zug pa'i thog ma shing stag lor 'khrungs par bshad /
de'i sngon rim gyis sde shog gi dbang sgyur dag rgyal phran chung ba'am rgyal phran sil ma'i lam lugs su gyur te /
sngon gyi lo rgyus dag las /
ma sangs spun dgus dbang bsgyur ba dang /
rgyal phran nyi shu rtsa lnga /
sil ma bzhi bcu /
yang rgyal phran bcu gnyis kyis dbang bsgyur bar bshad pa ltar la /
tha ma'i rgyal phran bcu gnyis po yang gcig gi 'og la gcig ma sgur bar phan tshun mi mthun par 'thab rtsod kyis dus 'da' bas /
'bangs la'ang dka' tshegs byung bar mngon te /
deb ther mkhas dga' las /
"rgyal phran de rnams 'thab rtsod gsod gcod dga' / /
legs nyes mi rtsi bkyon 'bebs btson rar 'jug " ces dang /
lde'u jo sras kyis mdzad pa'i lo rgyus las kyang /
"dus de tsam na rgyal phran bcu gnyis kyis dbang byed pa la rgyal phran che ba ma 'chams che ba'am gtso bo gang byed ma 'chams pa'i don nas bod kyi rje ma btub pa'i dus su zhang gsum bon bzhi la sogs pa dang /
shes pa mkhan mi bcu gnyis kyis /
mchid bgros nas rje btsal te /
" zhes gsungs pa ltar lo rgyus gzhan dag tu'ang yod do / /
gnya' khri btsan po'i yab la bshad tshul mi mthun pa du ma zhig yod mod /
mang bos bkur ba'i rgyal rgyud yin pa ban bon gyi yig cha khungs dag rnams mthun la /
de yang mang bos bkur ba'i rgyal bo'i rgyud las byung ba'i rgyal bo dmag brgya ba'i sras yin par deb ther dpyid kyi rgyal mo'i glu dbyangs sogs su bshad pa bzhin /
gleng gzhi bstan pa'i 'byung khungs khyung bo blo gros rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa las /
bon gzhung "mtho thog mdzod dang /
zhi khro rtsa 'grel dang gzhan sde'i lung kha cig mthun par /
u rgyan gyi rgyal bo dmag brgya ba'i sras yin par gsungs so" zhes dang /
yang de las /
"byams ma'i rgyal rabs las /
skyabs seng gi bu yin par bshad do / /
"zhes dang /
lde'u jo sras kyis mdzad pa'i lo rgyus las /
"gsang ba rgyal bo las chad pa ltar na /
gdung rgyud rigs gsum las /
che ba shAkya chen po /
'bring bo li tsa byi /
chung ba ri brag pa gsum las /
chung ba las dmag brgya ba'am skyabs seng las chad par 'dod do / /
"zhes gsungs pa ltar la /
gong gi de gsum sku mched kyi rigs su bshad pas 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud kyi lung bstan las "li tsa byi yi rigs su 'khrungs" gsungs pa dang yang mthun no / /
gnya' khri btsan po bod du byon lugs ni /
rgyal bo dmag brgya ba la sras mig mas 'gribs su yod pa g.yu'i smin ma can te /
g.yu mdog can /
so dung so 'khor mar yod pa /
lag pa 'khor lo'i yan lag can te ngang ba ltar 'brel ba /
rna ba la g.yung drung yod pa zhig 'khrungs pa yab kyis mthong nas /
lha 'dre'i sprul ba'am ltas ngan red snyam nas /
blon po dag la chur skyur cig ces bka' bsgos pas /
blon po rnams kyis sgam gyi nang du bcug nas chur 'phangs pa chus khyer nas /
yangs pa can gyi zhing ba rnams kyis zhing chu 'dren pa'i rka nang nas rnyed de kha phyes pas byis pa rigs mi 'dra ba zhig yod pa /
ngo mtshar skyes te blangs pa yul 'khor skyong gi dmag sdes thob kyang zer /
gang ltar cher skyes nas kho rang chu rka'i nang nas rnyed pa'i lo rgyus dang /
sngon gyi dmag 'khrug gi lo rgyus la sogs pa bshad pa'i rkyen gyis khyim la skyo ba skyes nas 'khor 'ga' zhig bcas yul gzhan du 'khyams /
mthar 'khor glu bu 'dzin mched drug dang bcas bod yul ri mtho la sa gtsang zhing bsil bar mthong nas der phebs te /
lha ri gyang tho'i rtse la slebs te gzigs pas /
yar lung gi yul 'di gtsang zhing yid du 'ong ba /
yar lha sham po'i gangs ri 'di mdzes shing lta na sdug par mthong ste /
lha ri rol bo'i rtse la gshegs nas /
btsan thang sgo bzhir bab pa'i skabs su /
bod 'bangs shes rigs gsal ba rnams rgyal phran dag ma 'chams pa'i 'thab rtsod sogs la skyo zhing /
bod spyi la dbang ba'i rgyal bo dbang thang can zhig yod na snyam du gleng mol mchid bgros byed bzhin pa yin te /
lde'u jo sras kyis mdzad pa'i bsgrags pa bon lugs bshad pa'i skabs las /
"rgyal phran che ba ma 'chams nas bod kyi rje ma btub pa'i dus su /
zhang gsum bon bzhi la sogs pa dang /
shes pa mkhan mi bcu gnyis kyis /
mchid bgros nas rje btsal te /
"zhes bshad pa ltar ro / /
de nas yon tan can gyi mi bcu gnyis kyis gnas der phyugs skyong zhing bsdad yod pa dang 'phrad /
gzugs byad lta bas chog mi shes par mthong nas ngo mtshar skyes te khyed gang nas 'ongs dris kyang /
khong 'khor dang bcas pas bod skad mi go stabs /
gnam la mdzub mo ker bas /
'di ni gnam las bab pa'i lha red do zer zhing /
'di ni bod kyi rgyal bor 'os zer nas shing gis khyogs shig bzos te gnya' bar khur nas gdan drangs /
bod 'bangs thams cad kyis lha las chad pa'i ngo mtshar can du bzung ste thams cad kyis bkur sti zhus shing rgyal bor bkur bas dbang thang cher gyur te rgyal phran bcu gnyis dbang du bsdus /
thog mar gnya' bar khri bcas nas gdan drangs pas /
mtshan la gnya' khri btsan por gsol /
pho brang yu bu bla mkhar brtsigs /
rgyal bo la snga ba gnya' khri btsan po /
yul la snga ba yar lung sog ka grong la snga ba phying ba stag rtse /
mkhar la snga ba yu bu bla mkhar zhes grags pa byung ngo / /
de'i skabs su khong gis dbang du bsdu bya'i rgyal phran bcu gnyis ni /
mchims rje tun hong du ne'u 'gu yod ces bya ba la blon po snang dang ding zhes pas byas pa dang gcig zhang zhung yul na rje legs snya shur zhes bya bar blon po rma dang ra sangs tun hong du stong los ma tse kyis byas pa dang gnyis /
myang ro phyed dkar na rje thod dkar zhes bya ba la blon po gnang zhes pas byas pa dang gsum /
gnubs yul gling dgu na rje dmigs pa tun hong du gnub rje sris ma zhes bya bar blon po rme'u dang 'bro zhes pas byas pa dang bzhi /
nyang ro sham por rje lo rngam rdzi 'grom tun hong du lo ma gyi zhes bya ba la blon po shes nyis zhes pas byas pa dang lnga /
kyi ri ljon tun hong du ljang sngon na rje kyi rje rmang bo zhes bya ba la blon po ngam dang 'bro tun hong du she'u dang sug gnyis zhes pas byas pa dang drug ngam shod khra snar tun hong du ngas po'i khra sum zhes rje khri 'phrang sum zhes bya ba la blon po mgar dang gnyan zhes pas byas pa dang bdun /
'ol phu spang mkhar du rje zing rje thon phreng tun hong du 'ol rje'i zin brang tsha zhes bya ba la blon po rdog dang sbas tun hong du rngo dang dbas zhes pas byas pa dang brgyad /
sribs yul gyi ral gong du rje brang rje gong nam zhes bya ba la blon po sprad zhugs zhes pas byas pa dang dgu /
kong yul khre sna na rje kar po tug ces bya ba la blon po mkhar ba zhes pas byas pa dang bcu /
nyang yul rnam gsum na rje nyang btsun glang rgyal zhes bya ba la blon po phug dang ngo rje zhes pas byas pa dang bcu gcig 'gas yul gru bzhi na rje 'gas rje mang bo rgyal zhes bya ba la blon po rlangs skam gnyis kyis byas pa dang bcu gnyis so / /

mgar g.yul bzang kho rang yang shi la khad byas /
nor rnams kyang zad de phyir log pas /
rgyal bo'i thugs dgongs ma 'grub /
'' ces gsungs so / /
de nas blon po chen po gnyal thu mi snang grags kyi bu thu mi a nu zhes bya ba /
phyis su thon mi sam+b+ho Ta zhes grags pa de nyid la grogs po khrel yod pa'i lo gzhon bcu drug dang bcas pa la gser dang rta drel sogs dngos skyes phun sum tshogs pa gnang nas rgya gar du mngags pa yin te /
smyu gu'i bstan bcos 'phrul gyi sgron me las /

zhes dang /
zur mkhar blo gros rgyal bos mdzad pa'i shes bya spyi'i khog dbug las /

rang cag la de lta bu med pas /
dman pa'i grangs su 'gro ba dang /

de ltar lho kha gnyal zhes bya ba'i yul gyi blon po thu mi snang grags kyi bu gzhon nu blo gsal zhing gzhung drang ba a nu zhes bya ba de grogs dang bcas rgya gar du yi ge slob tu brdzangs /

dga' bsu rgya chen po byas /

des na de ltar smras pa ni khyab pa ma nges pa'i rtags sbyor ro / /
mdor na bod kyi lo rgyus nang du yod pas yod go mi chod la /
mi rigs gzhan gyi lo rgyus nang du med pas med go chod ces ma smra zhig ces thal mo sbyar nas gsol lo / /
gzhan yang mang srong mang btsan gyi dus 'dir /
rgya nag gi sa khongs su yod pa'i thu lu hun zhes pa'i mi rigs rnams phar 'ded kyi ched du dpung chen bsags /
de'i don du mgar stong btsan gru gu'i yul du lo brgyad bzhugs zer yang /
mgar stong btsan de'i sngon nas gshegs tshar ba gong du bshad pa ltar ro / /
bod dpung gis thu lu hun phan par byas /
de rjes bod kyis dri ma 'khol zhes pa'i sa gnas su dmag gi rten gzhi chen po zhig btsugs /
thu lu hun rnams kyis bod kyi rgyal bo'i chab 'bangs su bka' brtsi khrims 'khur zhu rgyu'i mna' tshig phul 'dug de rjes bod dmag snga ram zhes pa'i sa char song nas an sha'i dmag sde bzhi blangs /
rgya nag gi zhu'i ring go'i zer ba'i dmag dpon gyis dmag 'bum phrag gcig khrid nas 'ongs te bod la 'thab kyang pham nyes chen po byung stabs /
rgya nag rgyal bos kho'i dmag spyi'i go gnas phab bo / /
de rjes bod kyi rgyal bo mang srong mang btsan gyis blon po 'dzin 'dzin zhes pa rgya'i skad yig shes pa zhig yod pa rgya nag tu sa mtshams skor 'dri zhib tu mngags /
rgya rgyal gyis mthong chen gyis sne len mdzad pa sogs la brten re zhig mtha' mtshams su zing 'khrug ma byung ba 'dra /
'on kyang lo drug tsam gyi rjes su yang bod dmag gis rgya'i yul gru shan co dang ko co zer ba gnyis bcom ste nor rdzas rnams bod yul du drangs /
de 'phral rgya rgyal gyis srid blon li'u jan go zer ba dpung bcas dang /
gzhan yang ta'o hos dang /
li li yu zer ba'i dmag dpon bcas lan cha'o la btang /
dmag dpung de tsho ma slebs gong bod dmag gis grong khyer e cha'o dang /
mi kong /
tang ling sogs kyang bcom par brten grong khyer mang bo bod 'og tu shor /
rgya rgyal gyis dmag dpon tsho'i go gnas phab /
slar yang srid don drung yig chen mo lis cin wan la dmag spyi'i go gnas sprad thog ce nan zhing chen dang shan nan zhing chen nas dmag bsnan te 'ongs nas long cir yod pa'i bod dmag la rgol nas pham par byas /
yang bskyar dmag snon dang bcas bod kyi blon po mgar btsan gnyan ldem bu bzhugs pa'i sa cha ko ko nor te mtsho sngon du dpung 'jug byas skabs rgya'i dmag dpon li'u shan li zer ba dmag thog der bsad pas dmag rnams phyir bros /
slar yang lis cin wan gyi 'og gi dmag dpon ha'i chi chang chi zer bas dmag khrid de bod kyi dmag sgar thog mtshan 'gebs byas nas bod dmag re zhig kha gtor tsam las /
bod dmag 'ded ma thub 'dug 'di dag spe lo Ta zhes pa'i lo rgyus nang du yod 'dug go / /
mang srong mang btsan 'das nas zhag bdun song mtshams /
lo der de'i sras 'dus srong mang bo rje rlung nam 'phrul gyi rgyal bo sgrags phur 'khrungs /
sras de dgung lo gsum la ma slebs bar du yab gshegs pa gsang rgya byas zer mkhan yod mod /
khungs rnam dag yod med ma shes /
nar son nas rgyal bor mnga' gsol /
mchims bza' btsan me tog btsun mor bsus /
mgar btsan gnyan ldem bu dang dbas ta ra khong lod gnyis kyis blon byas /
rgyal khams dbang du bsdus /
rgyal bo 'di'i ring la rtsal bo che'i mi bdun byung ba ni /
rngog ring la nag pos glang bo che'i phru gu theg rngog gling khams kyis g.yag grus po che theg gnon rgyal mtshan gyis mda' ste kha mas bya khra'i sked pa bcad /
dbas rgod ldongs btsan gyis mig rgyang gsum la mda' rgyang slebs /
'gos g.yag chung gis sha ba'i rlid bu bye mas bkang ba klad la bskor /
cog ro 'brong shor gyis 'brong thur du rgyug pa gyen la 'then /

de'i mchan las /

zhes gsungs pa ltar /
mgar btsan gnyan ldem bu sogs mgar sku mched bzhi rgya bod kyi sa mtshams su bzhugs te g.yul bkyes nas dgra pham zhing so mtshams srung ba'i bya ba byas stabs rgya'i lo rgyus nang du'ang 'di bzhi grags che bar yod 'dug go / /

ja 'thung byed kyi dkar yol /
dar snod dang dar tshe zhes bya ba bod rang gis bzos pa'i lo rgyus yid tshang mkhas pa dga' byed du gsal /
gzhan yang rol mo'i bye brag sna tshogs dar bar bshad do / /

'das lo brgya phrag brgyad pa'i nang tha'i rgyal bos bod la mgo btags /

zhes yod la /
de 'jang yul yin par bshad /
des na rgya'i yig cha'i nang /

bdun pa /

'bro chu bzang 'or ma gsum gyis byas /
gangs te se nas paN+Di ta sangs rgyas gsang ba dang sangs rgyas zhi ba gnyis gdan drangs kyang ma 'drongs /

brag dmar ke ru /

ces gsungs /
'di ni a rab kyi sa khongs red zer mkhan yod do / /

de nar son nas khab ran pa na /

de len rgyur blon 'bangs kha 'chams /

rgya'i deb ther las /
rgya rje 'khor dang bcas pas kong mkhar chen po zhing phed han gyi bar du skyel thung mdzad /
mkhar de'i nyes can thar du bcug btson grol btang dmag dang ldab nor khral lo gcig la med par byas /
mkhar de'i ming yang gyim shing hen zhes btags /
rgyal bus bod du rta brgyugs pas rtas bsgyur te 'das /

de'i tshe btsun mo che ba sna nam bzas /
"nga la rgyal bo'i gdung rgyud lus la yod do / /
"zhes rdzun smras te /
rgya mo bza' la khri srong lde btsan pho brang brag dmar du 'khrungs ma thag rgya mo'i rtsar byung /
shin tu blo nye ba ltar byas nas rgya mo'i bu chung phrogs te /
nga rang la skyes pa yin no zhes bsnyon byas so / /
der rgya mos rang gi nu ma bstan /
smre sngags bton /
cho nges bos kyang ma btang /
blon po sbran /

gos dang /
me tog gi phreng ba rnams khyer 'ongs so / /

de ltar khri srong lde btsan rgya bza'i bu yin par lo rgyus khungs dag rnams mthun par ma zad rgya bod gnyis char la yongs su grags shing mthun pa yin la /
khrin te rdzong gi lha khang ljang khu'i dkar chag rgya yig gi nang du'ang de ltar bris pa bdag gis mthong /
'on kyang /
tun hong gi gter yig nang du sna nam bza'i sras yin par bshad pa ni /
sna nam dbang che phyogs kyi phyogs lhung gi gtam rgyun ma dag pa zhig bris pa 'dra ste /
lo tshigs kyang gud nas bsgrig tu med do / /
yang lo gcig lon pa'i byis pas gtam de 'dra smra ba la thugs dogs za ba ni thugs rin chen gyi bu ga dog par mngon te /
khye'u la la lo gcig lon tsam nas 'gro bzhud dang smra brjod dag pa dang /
la la lo gsum bzhi lon yang da dung gtam mi 'chol ba lta bu sna tshogs shig deng dus su'ang yod par ma zad /
dmigs bsal can rna shes kyis yig gzugs 'dzin pa dang /
rkang 'og gi lus shes kyis yig gzugs 'dzin pa lta bu du ma zhig deng dus yod pa par dang bcas tshags par thog tu bkram pa dang /
dper na yus mas la sgrung 'bab pa lta bu mngon sum du gyur pa mang /
chos lugs rmongs dad du brtsi zhing tshan rig la yid ches pa ni sngon thon yin bsams mod /

thugs zur la phog na bzod par gsol lo / /

brgyad pa /
khri srong lde btsan gyi skor /
de nas khri srong lde btsan dgung lo bcu gsum thog rgyal sar 'khod mod /

stag ra klu gong sogs dbang che bas /
rgyal bo'i thugs 'dod ma grub /
rgyal bo'i thugs dgongs ni /
yab mes kyi dus ltar chos byed 'dod kyang /
ma zhang gis chos byed mi chog pa'i khrims bu chung bcas /
jo bo shAkya mu ne bye them du sbas /

rgya gar du skyel bar btang /

rgyal bo nar son pa na chos la dga' ba'i blon po 'gos khri bzang dang /
zhang nyams bzang sogs dang gros byas nas /
'gos kyis blo thabs phud de /
ma zhang gson por dur du bcug stag ra klu gong byang phyogs su spyugs /
jo bo mang yul nas gdan drangs te 'phrul snang gtsug lag khang du bzhugs /
sang shis rgya nag nas spyan drangs pa'i chos po ti rnams rgyal bo la phul /
sba gsal snang mngags te mkhan chen zhi ba 'tsho spyan drangs /
slar yang mkhan po'i zhal bkod bzhin slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas spyan drangs /
dpal bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs /
mkhan slob gnyis kas rab gnas mdzad /
mkhan po'i drung du sad mi mi bdun rab tu byung /
der mthud rab tu byung ba mang bo thon /
khams yas mas rnams su chos kyi grwa bcu gnyis btsugs /
yer ba dang mchims phur sgom grwa btsugs /
lo paN rnams kyis sngags mtshan nyid kyi chos phal mo che bsgyur zhing 'chad nyan gyis gtan la 'bebs pa'i zhabs tog bsgrubs pa ste sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa ches cher dar bar mdzad do / /
de rjes rgya nag nas hwa shang ma hA ya na byung ste /
tsen min dang don min te /

stag sgra klu gong 'di byang phyogs su rgyang 'phud gtong rgyu'i stag ra klu gong dang mi gcig lha bzang klu dpal rnams dmag 'bum phrag gnyis dang bcas la rgya nag phyogs su dpung 'jug dgos pa'i bka' stsal ba bzhin khong tshos rgya'i grong khyer cing cor dpung 'jug byas /
de ga'i spyi khyab ko hi zer bas bod la mgo btags /
de rjes spin ca'o nang khul gyi grong khyer phan si hun yang blangs /

bod dmag rnams myur shugs dang drag shugs ngang nas /

dga' ston sogs byas /

zhes bshad yod 'dug 'di'i skabs kyi lo rgyus ni khri srong lde btsan gyi sku dus /

gzhan yang khri srong lde btsan gyi skabs su rma chu'i byang phyogs su skyen po mi dgu ste /

su ci'u gsum yin /
lhor bram ze'i yul dang /
byang hor gyi yul te /
de rnams bskor ba la dpag tshad stong phrag mang bo yod pas /
bod las dpa' ba dang /
rtul phod pa rgya'i gong ma hAn dang /
g.yu dang /
lci'u la sogs pa'i dus su'ang ma byung ba yin no / /
zhes rgya'i deb ther las bshad 'dug pa ltar ro / /
chos rgyal de la btsun mo tshe spong bza' me tog sgron /
'bro bza' byang chub sgron /
pho yong bza' rgyal mo btsun dang gsum yod /
gzhan gnyis la sras med /
tshe spong bza' la sras gsum yod pa'i che ba mu ne btsan po la rgyal sa gtad de /
rgyal bo rang nyid zung mkhar du sgom sgrub la zhugs /
de'i phyi lo shing glang lor zung mkhar du sku gshegs /
bang so mu ra ri la brtsigs so / /
rgyal dbang gis sras 'bring ba mu tig btsan po yin pa dang /
mu tig btsan po dang sad na legs mjing yon gcig yin par gsungs pa ni /
rgyal bo'i bka'i thang yig la brten pa yin la /
thang yig la nor 'khrul mang ba dpa' bo gtsug lag 'phreng ba sogs kyis bshad cing /
rgyal dbang rang gis kyang du klu la'i gos bzang du /
thang yig gi lo tshigs sogs bsgrig thabs med ces /
ma dag par gsungs /
des na lo rgyus mang che bar mu tig btsan po dang /
sad na legs mi gcig par bshad pas /
de ltar don la gnas snyam zhing /
mu tig btsan po zhes pa zhig deb ther mang che bar mi 'byung la /
gal te yod na /
sras che ba yin pa la /
chung dus nas gshegs pa 'dra zhes mkhas pa 'ga' zhig gsung /
sad na legs kyi mtshan la khri lde srung btsan du 'chad pa ni sgra sbyor bam gnyis ma mthong ba'i skyon no / /
gsungs mod /
sgra sbyor bam gnyis su de ral ba can gyi mtshan byas pa ni yi ge ma dag pa shin tu gsal te /
de'i skor la bu ston chos 'byung /
deb dmar gsar rnying gnyis /
deb sngon /
mkhas pa'i dga' ston /
bka' gtsigs chen mo /
me long ma /
sa skya'i chos 'byung /
klong chen chos 'byung /
gser gyi shing rta /
rdo ring yi ge /
tun hong gi gter yig sogs gcig mthun red do / /
dgu ba /
mu ne btsan po dang sad na legs kyi skor /
mu ne btsan po ni chu stag lor 'khrungs /
yab rgyal bo ma gshegs gong rgyal sras bzhugs /
rgyal dbang gis deb dmar dang /
me long ma dang mthun par /
mu ne btsan bos lo gcig dang zla ba dgur rgyal srid bzung zhes bshad /
deb ther dmar bo gsar ma'i nang /
ki kaM spyan snga'i chos 'byung sogs dang mthun par /
lo bdun dang zla ba dgur rgyal srid bzung bar bshad /
thang yig gsar ma'i nang du'ang lo grangs 'di dang mthun 'dug phyag las sogs la dpag na de dag snyam /
btsun mo ru yong bza' mdo rgyal khab tu bzhes /
dge ba bcu'i khrims bzung ste /
sde snod gsum gyi mchod pa rgya chen po btsugs /
'bangs rnams dbul phyug mi mnyam par mthong nas /
'bangs kyi dbul phyug lan gsum gyi bar snyoms par mdzad mod /
sngar bzhin dbul phyug mi mnyam par gyur /
lo paN rnams kyis sngon gyi sbyin 'bras yin gsungs pas /
lhag par rnam dkar la yid ches par gyur /
mnga' thang yab mes kyi dus bzhin rgyas te byang du dpung chen bshams pa sogs mdzad pa dang phyag rjes rgya che mod /
yab kyi btsun mo pho yong bza' rgyal mo btsun zer ba de lo gzhon cing gzugs byad mdzes pas /
btsun mo gzhan gyis phrag dog byed yong snyam du yab kyi thugs 'phreng bar gyur te /
zung mkhar du byon dus /
sras la gtad gnyer mdzad de sras kyi khab tu bzhes yod pa la /
yum tshe spong bza' phrag dog skyes nas /
yab rgyal bo grongs dus /
pho yong bzas rgyan ma bkrol /
mya ngan ma byas zhes snyad btags te /
gshed ma bskos nas gsod du btang tshe /
sras mu ne btsan pos srung skyob byas stabs gsod ma thub /
yum ma dga' nas rang sras mu ne btsan po la dug drangs te dgung lo nyer dgu'i thog pho brang yu bur grongs so / /
bang so ni mes ag tshom gyi bang so'i g.yas ngos kyi mdun na yod do / /
'bring bo mu tig btsan po ni /
sngar yab rgyal bo dang blon po zhang gnyis dmag srid sogs kyi don la bka' bgros skabs sgo srung la zhang rgyal tsha lha snang gi bu dbu ring bzhag pa la /
sras mu tig bka' bgros sar 'gro grabs byed skabs /
dbu ring gis bkag pas /
sras kyis chu gri bsnun te bkums /
blon po 'gos kyis zhal lce dga' gsum dang sdig gsum bcad de /
sras mu tig sa mthar spyugs pa /
rgyal sar 'don rgyu byas te spyan drangs mod /
lam du sna nam pas chibs dkrogs te lhung nas rta grir 'das /
de nas sras chung ba khri lde srong btsan sad na legs mjing yon rgyal sar bton /
blon po mkhas pa bran kha dpal gyi yon tan /
nyang ting 'dzin bzang bo /
zhang mdo khri sher /
ngan lam khri rgyal bzhis blon gtso bo byas te rgyal srid bskyangs /
blon dang bo gnyis rten rab byung yin mod nyams myong che bas blon du bskos pa red gsungs /
rgyal bo des rgyal khams la dbang bsgyur te dge bcu'i khrims bcas shing /
yab mes kyis bzhengs pa'i gtsug lag khang rnams la mchod pa rgya chen po phul ba dang /
paN Di ta du ma spyan drangs /
lo paN rnams kyis sngon ma 'gyur ba'i mdo dang bstan bcos mang bo bsgyur /
skyid shod du dkar chung rdo rje dbyings kyi lha khang bzhengs /
blon 'bangs thams cad la dam pa'i chos mi zhig cing /
dkon mchog gsum bla mar bya ba'i khrims bsgrags shing /
mna' bor /
bka' gtsigs kyi yi ge mang bo bris te rgyas btab nas mdzod du bzhag rdo ring la brkos pa sogs mkhas pa'i dga' ston du zhib par yod /
rgyal bo de'i ring la dkar chag 'phang thang ma dang /
dkar chag ldan dkar ma bzhengs par gsungs /
'di dang mu ne btsan po'i dus su rgya dang dmag 'dren res thengs kha shas byas pa dang /
nub phyogs su 'brel ba rgya chen byas /
me long mar /
sad na legs kyi sras ldeng khri /
de la sras lnga byung bar bshad pa ni lo rgyus gzhan gang dang mi mthun pas ma dag pa red /
rgyal bo 'di me bya lor 'das /
lo der ral ba can khrir bkod do / /
bcu ba /
khri ral dang dar ma sogs kyi skor /
rgyal bo khri lde srong btsan sad na legs mjing yon la sras gtsang ma /
dar ma /
ral ba can /
lha rje /
lhun 'grub ste lnga /
dar ma 'u dum btsan chu lug lor 'khrungs /
khri gtsug lde btsan ral ba can me khyi lor 'khrungs /
lha rje /
lhun 'grub gnyis chung du nas 'das /
gtsang ma rab tu byung /
dar ma blun zhing spyod pa ngan la sdig spyod la dga' bas /
spyod pa ngan na rigs don med /
ces gsungs pa ltar /
rgyal bor mi 'os pa shes nas /
blon po nyams myong can rnams kyis gros thog nas /
khri gtsug lde btsan ral ba can rgyal sras bkod /
btsun mo dpal gyi ngang tshul khab tu bzhes /
bran kha dpal yon sogs kyis blon po byas te /
rgyal khams la dbang bsgyur /
'u shang rdo'i dpe med bkra shis dge 'phel gyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs /
paN Di ta mang bo spyan drangs te lo paN rnams kyis mdo rgyud bstan bcos mang bo bsgyur /
lo paN rnams kyis sngar bsgyur pa rnams la dag bcos dang /
skad gsar bcad kyis gtan la phab ste /
bye brag rtogs byed che 'bring chung gsum mdzad /
'bring ba la sgra sbyor bam gnyis zer /
'di'i dus su yang rgya dang dbon zhang ma mthun par /
bod dmag khri tsho mang bo drangs te /
rgya yul gyi mkhar mang bo bcom pa'i skabs /
bod kyi dge 'dun pa rnams dang /
rgya'i btsun pa rnams kyis bar byas nas bka' mol gyi mtshams sbyar te dbon zhang mthun par mdzad /
rgya'i gung gu rme rur rdo ring btsugs te rgya bod kyis mtshams su bcad nas /
phan tshun gnyis kas sa mtshams las phyi rol tu brgal te dmag gi g.yul bshams pa sogs mi byed pa'i dpang du lha klu gnyan po bzhag ste bro bor ba'i yi ge lha sa dang /
rgya rje'i pho brang /
gung gu rme ru gsum gyi rdo ring la bris /
dus der rgya bod gnyis mthun zhing 'brel ba bzang bas /
gnam la nyi zla zung gcig dang /
sa la btsan po dbon zhang zhes gleng /
dbon zhang zhes pa'i don /
sngar mes ag tshom gyis rgya bza' gyim shing kong jo blangs pa la sras khri srong lde btsan 'khrungs stabs /
bod kyi btsan po rjes ma rnams rgya'i tsha rgyud du gyur stabs /
bod la dbon zer ba tsha bu'i ming /
rgya la zhang zer /
de'i dus kyi chings yig skor gyi lo rgyus rgya'i mkhas pa wang cung zer bas brtsams pa'i deb cig gi nang du gsal bo yod zer /
rdo ring gi ngos yi ge ni gzhan gyis bshus pa'i bu yig da lta'ang yod /
gung gu rme ru ni ka ci'i mchod rten dkar bo yod sa de red zer zhing /
mchod rten 'di sangs rgyas 'od srung dus kyi mchod rten zhig yin zer ba dang /
bdag cag gi ston pa'i 'phel gdung bzhugs pa'i mchod rten yin zer ba'i lo rgyus ci rigs snang /
zhes gung thang bstan pa'i sgron me'i rnam thar las gsungs /
'on kyang mchod rten de lo bcu phrag 'ga'i sngon du bshigs nas /
der chu mdzod cig bzos yod /
da lta slar yang mchod rten zhig ri khar bzhengs yod 'dug rgyal bo 'dis yab mes dus kyi khrims yig rnams gzhir bzhag nas bka' khrims legs par bcas te /
ngan pa la chad pa gcod pa /
bzang ba la bya dga' ster ba /
mtho ba'i gnya' nas gnon cing /
dma' ba thabs kyis skyong ba'i srol bzang phyogs kun tu khyab ste /
khyim na bag dro mi ni khong dal /
phyugs ni lo dang zla ba na sdud /
mi nyal mis slong /
'bri yan sna med /
sgo la khyi med /
rje byams /
'bangs gus /
grogs gzhung bzang /
gnyen sha tsha /
pho ni dpa' bo dang /
mo mdzangs la chas bzang /
bod 'bangs bde skyid kyi dpal la gnas /
rgyal bo'i ral ba'i sne la dar yug btags nas /
de'i steng du dge 'dun bzhugs su bcug pa sogs dkon mchog gsum la gus 'dud lhur blangs /
dge 'dun re la mi khyim bdun re phul to / /
rgyal bo 'dis bkas bcad gsum mdzad pa ni /
skad gsar bcad kyi bkas bcad dang /
'dul ba gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i sde ba las /
sde ba gzhan gyi 'dul ba mi bsgyur bar bkas bcad /
gsang sngags ma rgyud rnams mi bsgyur bar bkas bcad pa ste gsum mo / /
lha tho tho ri nas 'di'i bar la skyid pa'i gdung rabs phyed dang bcu gsum zhes zer /
mu ne btsan po yun thung bas phyed du brtsis /
mang srong ma bgrangs /
mes ag tshom nas 'di'i bar la shin tu skyid pa'i gdung rabs lnga zhes snga rabs la grags so / /
de nas /
blon po 'ga' zhig gi sems rgyud phrag dog gis dkrugs te /
blon chen po bran kha dpal yon dang btsun mo dpal gyi ngang tshul gnyis mthun zhes phra ma bcug nas /
ban de bran kha dpal yon bkums /
btsun mo gzhi med kyi phra ma des yi mug nas pho brang thog nas lcebs te shi /
btsan po khri ral dgung lo sum cu so drug thog lcags bya lor pho brang ma zhar nyi ma la bzhugs skabs /
dbas to re dang /
cog ro legs sgra gsang stabs su 'ongs nas zhal ltag par bsgyur te bkrongs so / /
bang so don mkhar mda'i g.yon phyogs su brtsigs so / /
de nas 'u dum btsan rgyal sar bzhag dbas rgyal to re dang /
sbas stag sna /
nya nam rgya tsha khri srung sogs blon po byas /
btsan po 'di ni chung dus nas gzugs ba lang gi sha tshugs dang 'dra zhing /
blo rtul la rgyud gyong bas /
'bangs rnams kyis glang dar ma zhes btags /
ming dngos la 'u dum btsan zer /
rgya'i lo rgyus rgya'i lo tsA ba ba hu gyang ju zer bas bod yig tu bsgyur ba las /
"rgyal bo 'di chang la dga' zhing spyod pa ngan pas /
bod kyi rgyal khams thams cad 'khrugs /
si ha ce'u la bod 'bangs dbang ba'i ri brtsigs yod pa 'gyel /
klu chu zhag gsum gyen la log ltas ngan byung zhing rgyal khams zhig pa yin no /
" /
zhes bshad do / /
de nas glang dar kho rang blo rmongs shing yon tan med par ma zad /
yon tan can la snying nas mi dga' bas /
chos byas pa bkra mi shis zer nas /
rma rin chen mchog dang /
nyang ting 'dzin sogs lo tsA ba chen po mang bo bkrongs /
paN Di ta rnams sa mthar bskrad pa dang /
la la rang rang so so'i yul du bros /
rab tu byung ba la la sa mthar bros /
ma thar ba rnams khyim sar phab /
mi nyan pa rnams bsad /
la la khrid nas rgyal blon rnams kyis rta la 'bab 'dzeg byed tshe sgur du bcug nas stegs byas /
la la'i lag tu rnga gshang dang mgo la khyim sar phab pa'i rtags bya sgro btsugs nas ri dwags rngon du bcug khyim pa rnams zhwa'i thog tu bya sgro 'dzugs pa yin la /
rab byung dag gis gos brje byed ma rnyed kyang mgo la bya sgro btsugs nas khyim pa yin tshul byed dgos byung /
lha sa dang bsam yas bshas ra byas /
gtsug lag khang mang bo bshigs /
dpe cha rnams chu la skur ba dang me la sreg pa dang /
sa 'og tu gnon pa sogs byas /
'on kyang bsam yas ni rgyal sar cung thag ring bas ra sa'i gtsug lag khang lta bu'i gtsang dag byed ma thub par dpe cha mang bo shul du lus /
bod 'bangs rnams kyi 'tsho ba'ang nyin re bzhin je sdug la song /
blon po dang mngag gzhug pa sogs kyis sdig btsir bzod glags med pa byas pa sogs kyis sdug bsngal gyi gnas su bcar to / /
de'i tshe lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje ye ba brag lha ri na sgom byed kyin yod pa /
nyin gcig sgom khang phyi la phebs gzigs pas btsun pa'i mgo la bya sgro btsugs /
lag tu rnga gshang thogs te lings byed pa rngon mthong bas /
rgyal bos bstan pa bsnubs shing /
'bangs rnams sdug bsngal ba'i gnas la bcar bar shes nas /
snying rje chen po skyes te rgyal bo ma bsgral na 'bangs rnams sdug bsngal zhing /
rgyal bo rang nyid kyis kyang las ngan pa ches mang bo bsags nas dmyal bar ltung bar 'gyur ro dgongs nas /
rta zhon mda' gzhu thogs te rgyal bo gsod du chas /
de'i tshe rgyal bo gla ba'i tshal du mig mang rtse zhing 'dug pa'i thag nyer 'bangs 'dus te ngu 'bod byed cing khrom skor rgyal bo lags 'di 'dra'i bya ba ngan pa byed pa ni mi rigs so / /
yab mes kyi yig tshang dang dkor mdzod kyi sgrom bu rdo ring gi yi ge rnams la gzigs dang /
zhes ngu 'bod byas pa'i 'ur sgra rgyal bos thos nas sems mi bde bar /
yar 'gro mar 'gro byas te rdo ring gi rtsar slebs nas /
rdo ring gi yi ge klog gin yod skabs /
lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje slebs te /
rgyal bo la phyag 'bul khul gyis phu dung nang nas mda' gzhu blangs te lcags kyi mda' 'phangs pas /
rgyal bo'i snying gar phog ste tshe'i dus byas so / /
'dis rgyal srid lo drug la bzung /
me stag lor glang dar 'das so / /
'di la deb sngon dang sum pa'i chos 'byung du /
me 'brug la khri ral bkrongs /
dar ma khrir bzhag gsungs mod /
mkhas pa mang che bas lcags bya la ngos 'dzin /
phyis kyi zhib dpyod mkhan mang che bas phyi ma de dag par bshad /
gzhan yang bstan bsnubs lcags bya lo zhes mkhas pa kun mthun par gleng /
des na bstan bdag rgyal blon btsun mo dang bcas pa bkrongs /
bstan dgra rgyal blon dang bcas pa khrir 'gying nas /
bstan pa'i bsnyen bkur chad de /
bstan 'dzin la gnag pa'i lo de la bstan bsnubs lo zer dgos la /
mang che bas bstan bsnubs lcags bya lo zer ba dang yang mthun no / /
bcu gcig pa /
bod sil bur gyur pa sogs /
glang dar bsgral ba'i phyi lo me yos lor 'od srung dang yum brtan gnyis ka 'khrungs par bshad /
btsun mo chun ma tshe spong bza' btsan mo 'phan la sras gcig byung ba /
chen ma sna nam bzas 'phrog gam gsod ces dogs nas mtshan mor mar me'i 'od dang ma bral bar bsrungs pas mtshan la gnam lde 'od srung du thogs /
de'i tshe chen ma sna nam bzas kyang 'bangs dbul zhig la bu chung zhig nyos nas nga la yang bu chung zhig skyes zhes bstan pas /
blon po rnams kyis mdang skyes pa'i bu la so ni tsag tsig 'dug 'on kyang yum gyi bka' brtan du chug zer bas /
khri lde yum brtan du ming chags /
bu chung de gnyis nar son nas /
blon po rnams kyis phas chos bsnubs pas bkra mi shis pa byung song /
zhes bsnyad nas jo bo rnam gnyis dang byams pa chos 'khor ma spyan drangs te khri thog tu bzhugs su gsol /
mchod pa byas /
'on kyang bstan pa nar ma ni ma byung 'dug de nas glang dar gyi sras rtsod med gnam lde 'od srung dang /
dogs pa can khri lde yum brtan gnyis nang ma 'chams par /
yum brtan gyis dbu ru bzung /
'od srung gis g.yo ru bzung nas 'khrugs pa byas /
de'i rkyen gyis bod yul phal che ba'i sde ba dang shog kha'i nang ma 'chams par 'khrug rtsod byung /
yang glang dar gyi dus nas bod yongs su khral sogs mi 'tsham pa sna tshogs kyis mnar zhing /
rgyal khrims zhig pas 'tsho ba sogs gang sa nas dka' tshegs byung stabs /
'bangs rnams bod rgyal srid gzhung la mi dga' bar gyur /
glang dar gyi sras gnyis lo nyer gsum lon pa sa glang lo nas rim gyis kheng log byung /
thog mar dbas kho bzher legs steng zhes bya bas lag dpon byas te mdo smad du kheng log byung /
de nas dbu rur 'brong dang sbas kyi 'khrug pa la brten nas /
dbas lo pho lo chung zhes bya bas lag dpon byas te kheng log byung /
de nas g.yo rur zhang rje gsas sne btsan zer bas dpon g.yu sne zer ba bsad /
khyim kong mi drug gis lag dpon byas te 'od 'bar kheng log tu grags pa byas /
kheng log byas nas lo dgu ba me bya lor shud pu stag rtse sogs mi bzhis gros byas nas bang so rnams bgo bsha' brgyab phal cher brus /
gnyags kyis don mkhar mda' yi bang so brus /
shud pus seng ge can gyi bang so brus /
'phrul rgyal bang so greng 'phyos khu yis brus /
sngo bzher snyi bas thob kyang 'bru 'phror lus /
srong btsan bang so 'bro dang cog la thob kyang 'bru 'phror lus /
zhes yig rnying las bshad 'dug sras rtsod med gnam lde 'od srung de pho brang yu bu bla sgang du 'khrungs /
so dgu ba shing sbrul lor pho brang 'phang thang du 'das /
de'i sras mnga' bdag dpal 'khor btsan shing bya lor 'khrungs /
yab 'das nas rgyal sa mdzad /
sman lung sogs lha khang brgyad bzhengs kyang /
lo so gcig thog stag rtse gnyags kyis bkrongs /
de'i sras bkra shis brtsegs pa dpal dang /
skyid lde nyi ma mgon gnyis /
mi sde phal cher yum brtan la shor bas mnga' ris su bros /
mnga' ris kyi blon po zhang ba tshab rin chen sde dang /
cog ro legs sgra lha legs gnyis kyis bsnyen bkur zhus /
rgyal sras de gnyis spyod pa bzang zhing blo gros che bas mnga' ris kyi rgyal bor gyur /
spu rangs su sku mkhar nyi bzung brtsigs /
blon po gnyis kyi bu mo re btsun mor phul /
skyid lde nyi ma mgon dang btsun mo cog ro bza' la sras gsum 'khrungs pa'i che ba dpal lde nyi ma mgon yang zer /
rig pa mgon yang zer ba des mang yul bzung /
bkra shis mgon gyis spu rangs bzung /
lde gtsug mgon gyis zhang zhung bzung /
'di gsum la stod kyi mgon gsum zer /
chung ba lde gtsug mgon la sras 'khor re dang /
srong nge gnyis /
srong nges sku tshe'i stod la khab bzhes pas /
sras nA ga rA dza dang /
de wa rA dza gnyis 'khrungs /
sku tshe'i smad la rab tu byung bas mtshan la lha bla ma ye shes 'od ces grags /
khong gis mthon lding gi lha khang bzhengs pa dang /
khye'u blo rno ba nyi shu rtsa gcig rgya gar du rig pa'i gnas dang chos slob tu brdzangs /
lo chen rin bzang dang legs shes gnyis kyang 'di'i grangs yin /
rgyal bo khong yang chos dang rig pa'i gnas la shin tu mkhas /
paN Di ta warma gsum spyan drangs chos mang du bsgyur /
sku mched 'di gnyis sras rgyud dang bcas pa'i dus mnga' ris su 'bangs bde skyid dang ldan no / /
phyis su gar log dang ma 'grig nas /
gar log gis btson du bcug ste btson 'og nas 'das /
khong gi gcen po 'khor re la sras lha lde 'khrungs /
de la sras 'od lde /
pho brang zhi ba 'od /
btsun pa byang chub 'od dang gsum yod /
btsun pa byang chub 'od kyis jo bo rje spyan drangs pa sogs phyag rjes che ba sogs lo rgyus rnams su grags che /
de'i gcen 'od lde'i sras mnga' bdag rtse lde /
rngog lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab rgya gar sogs su phyi nang gi rig gnas slob tu phyin pa la /
mthun rkyen rgya chen mdzad /
mnga' ris su chos 'khor chen mo btsugs /
mnga' bdag rtse lde 'di'i sras 'bar lde /
de'i sras bkra shis lde /

g.yu ring /

de cher skyes dus /

'di rten rab byung /

de nas khong gis gdan sa mdzad de /

de yang sa skya paN Di tas mkhas pa'i bya ba 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis dus 'da' bar mdzad pas /

'dir hor rgyal gyi byung ba mdo tsam brjod na /
hor jing gir rgyal bo zhes grags pa'i dbang sdud can de rab byung gsum pa'i chu rta lo la skyes pa red zer /

byang phyogs u ru si dang /

de la bu lnga yod pa'i che ba ab to zer ba rang gi pha'i rgyal sar bsdad /

u go ta'i rgyal sar bkod /

de'i phyi lor go tan yang 'das /

'phags pa rin po che gong ma'i rgyal sar phebs /

sa skya'i dpon chen rnams kyang /

sa skya dang byang bdag ma mthun pas /
sa skya'i rgyab tu rin spungs pa langs te /
chu phag lor rin spungs pa'i dmag g.yas ru byang ba'i steng du chas pa'i tshe ngag dbang 'jig grags rang yang dpung bcas bsam 'grub rtser slebs /
lo de ga'i nang rin spungs pa rang gi zhabs 'bring ba chibs dpon du gtogs pa zhing shag pa tshe brtan rdo rje zer ba bsam rtse'i rdzong dpon byas nas yod pa des 'bangs gyen log byas te /
sras pad ma dkar bo bkrongs pa sogs rim gyis nyams rgud du gyur /
rin spungs pa yang dar ba'i tha ma rgud pas mjug bsdus so / /
bco lnga ba /
sde srid gtsang ba'i lo rgyus /
rin spungs pa'i rjes su /
sde srid gtsang bas bod la dbang bsgyur pa yin la /
'di la gtsang stod sde ba yang zer /
gtsang ba rgyal bo yang zer /
'di ni gnyags dz+nya na ku ma ra sogs kyi gdung rgyud yin zer /
gtsang rgyal gyi thog ma ni /
zhing shag pa tshe brtan rdo rje yin la /
kho ni rin spungs pa'i gnyen tshan du gtogs la /
rin spungs pa dang /
sne gdong ba gnyis ka'i zhabs 'bring gi khongs su bsdad /
rin spungs sde srid ngag dbang rnam rgyal gyi skabs su chibs dpon gyi las ka bzung /
de rjes las tshan du slebs te /
shangs dang /
myang smad kyi yong 'bab sdud mkhan lo mang bor byas /
sa sprel lor gzhis ka bsam 'grub rtse'i rdzong dpon gyi go gnas thob ste der bsdad /
rin spungs sde srid ngag dbang 'jig grags kyi skabs su /
khong gi gcen che ba pad ma dkar bo zhing shag pas bkrongs stabs /
rin spungs pas dmag drangs pa lam du ma song bar /
bsam 'grub rtse ba zhing shag pa tshe brtan rdo rjes 'bangs gyen log byas te /
rin spungs pa'i mnga' 'og nas bud /
me sbrul lor /
zhing shag pa tshe brtan rdo rjes /
shangs don rab pa'i sa sde rnams dpung shugs kyis blangs /
shing glang lor zhing shag pa rang nyid dmag dpon byas te /
pa snam lhun 'grub khyung rtse dang /
rdzong gsar phag mo ri rnams blangs /
slar me stag lo'i lo sar mtshams gtsang rin gnyis kyis myang stod smad du dmag 'khrug bslangs mthar /
pa snam rdzong yongs rdzogs gtsang bas thob /
zhing shag pa tshe brtan rdo rje gtsang gi rgyal bor gyur /
zhing shag pa la bu dgu byung ba las /
karma mthu stobs rnam rgyal /
kun spang lha dbang rdo rje /
karma bstan srung dbang bo 'di gsum gyis gtsang phyogs su dbang bsgyur 'dug sras gzhan gyi lo rgyus mi snang /
lha dbang rdo rje bsam 'grub rtse'i rgyal sar bsdad /
bstan srung dbang bo pa snam nor khyung rtser bsdad /
de rjes lha dbang rdo rje 'das rjes /
bstan srung dbang bo bsam 'grub rtse'i rgyal sar bsdad /
de 'das rjes /
de'i sras phun tshogs rnam rgyal lo bcu bzhi'i thog lcags phag lor srid dbang bzung /
de'i dus byi glang lo'i sde gzar zhes bya ba byung ste /
de ni chu byi lo dang /
chu glang lor phun tshogs rnam rgyal gyis mnga' ris rgyal bo dang /
lho ba byang ba rnams la dmag drangs nas mnga' 'og tu bcug pa de la zer /
kho bka' brgyud pa la mos khul byas mod /
'brug pa pad ma dkar bo'i yang sprul ngag dbang rnam rgyal dang dpag bsam dbang bo gnyis 'khrungs pa gdan sar gang 'god 'then 'khyer byung /
ngag dbang rnam rgyal gyis gtsang ba'i bka' chad phog dogs nas lho 'brug phyogs su bros byol byed dgos byung ba dang /
gtsang dmag 'brug pa'i thog tu lan gnyis btang ba sogs 'brug pa bka' brgyud dang 'gras pa byung /
'on kyang karma ba'i sbyin bdag byas te /
karma chos dbyings rdo rje la dbus gtsang gi bdag po'i bka' shog dang tham ga dmar nag byin /
jo nang tA ra na tha yang bla mar bsten /
karma ba la dad khul gyis dge lugs pa la shin tu sdang /
rab byung bcu ba'i sa rta lor dbus su dmag drangs nas sa lug lor se 'bras gnyis bcom /
dge 'dun rnams byang phyogs su ded /
skya ser brgya phrag mang bo bsad /
bkra shis lhun po'i rgyab ri'i kha nas sa rdo drangs te bkra shis lhun po dang /
gzhis ka rtse'i bar bka' brgyud kyi dgon pa gsar rgyag gi mkhar las byed skabs /
rbab rdo bsgril ba sogs paN chen rin po che dang bkra shis lhun po sogs la brnyas gtse byas pas 'o brgyal byung /
lcags bya lor sog dmag stong gnyis lhag slebs te /
gtsang dmag dang 'thab nas gtsang dmag pham /
paN chen rin po che sogs kyis bar 'dum mdzad /
se 'bras kyi mchod gzhis tshur sprad /
grub mtha' bsgyur ba rnams dang sa ris shor ba sogs rang babs su slog lcags lug la phun tshogs rnam rgyal 'das nas /
sras karma bstan skyong khrir bkod zer /
gtsang rgyal gyis rgyal ba paN chen gnyis dang /
bkra shis lhun po dang se 'bras dge gsum sogs dang /
skyid shod sde ba stag rtse ba sogs la yang yang brnyas gtse byas /
skyid shod sde ba sog yul du bros /
rgyal dbang lnga ba chen po'i pha hor bdud 'dul rab brtan btson du bcug pa btson zhabs nas 'das /
stag rtse sde ba sogs mi chen 'gas gros thog nas sog po o rod jun gar gyi dpon gu shrI khAng la rogs zhu mi byed ka med byung /
gu shrI bstan 'dzin khAng gis chu rta lor gtsang ba'i srid gzhung rtsa med btang ste /
bod ljongs yongs kyi srid dbang dga' ldan pho brang ba'i lag tu 'byor /
thog ma'i char karma ba'i phyogs nas nang 'khrug phran chags byung mod /
de ma thag zhi ste /
ser skya drag zhan thams cad sos bder gnas chog pa byung ngo / /
bcu drug pa /
dga' ldan pho brang ba'i lo rgyus /
gtsang ba'i srid dbang mjug bsdus rjes rgyal dbang lnga ba'i dus nas dga' ldan pho brang bas bod la dbang bsgyur /
des na thog mar rgyal dbang sku phreng rim byon gyi lo rgyus mdo tsam shes dgos pas mdor bsdus shig brdzod par bya ste /
rgyal dbang sku phreng dang bo dge 'dun grub pa /
de yang paN chen dge 'dun grub pa sku phreng dang bor byas nas sku phreng rim par brtsi dgos la /
de yang dge 'dun grub pa dpal bzang bo ni /
rab byung bdun pa'i lcags lug lor gtsang shab stod gur mo zhes pa'i yul du 'khrungs /
dgung lo bcu bzhi'i thog snar thang chos sder phebs /
rab tu byung /
slob gnyer dang gsan bsam rgya cher gnang ste mkhas grags 'bar /
shing lug lor rje tsong kha pa dang mjal te /
slob ma'i gtso bo zhig tu gyur /
rab byung brgyad pa'i me yos lor bkra shis lhun po phyag 'debs mdzad /
dgon sde der 'chad nyan mdzad de yun ring bzhugs /
paN chen dge 'dun grub ces mtshan snyan rgyas /
de rjes bkra shis lhun po'i gdan sa 'dzin mkhan rnams la paN chen zhes mtshan thogs /
tshad ma rigs rgyan sogs gsung rtsom mang /
dgung lo gya bzhi'i thog gsungs mod gya drug yin dgos 'dra /
rab byung brgyad pa'i shing rta lor sku 'das so / /
rgyal dbang sku phreng gnyis pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho /
de'i phyi lo shing lug lor gtsang rta nag tu 'khrungs /
dge 'dun grub pa'i yang srid du ngos 'dzin mdzad de bkra shis lhun por spyan drangs /
karma ba la sprul sku ngos 'dzin pa'i srol 'di'i sngon nas yod mod /
dge lugs pa la sprul sku ngos 'dzin pa'i thog ma 'di ba yin /
de dus rin spungs pa don yod rdo rjes dbang bsgyur ba'i skabs yin pas sde gzar mang bo byung /
shing yos lor rgyal ba dge 'dun rgya mtsho 'bras spungs su phebs /
bsnyen par rdzogs /
lo 'dir skyid shod du snang rtse khu dbon rkyen lam du btang /
sa rta lor rin spungs dmag lha sar drangs /
snel ba dpon ngag dbang lhun po mched gnyis skyor mo lung du phud /
de ga'i rdzong gzhis tshang ma rin spungs don yod rdo rjes blangs /
lo 'di nas bzung sa stag bar du lo nyi shu'i ring la se 'bras kyi dge 'dun pa rnams lha sa smon lam chen mor phebs mi chog pa byung /
sa sbrul rnams lha sa smon lam chen mor phebs mi chog pa byung /
sa sbrul lor rgyal ba dge 'dun rgya mtshos rgyal me tog thang gi dgon pa btab /
lha mo'i bla mtsho'i gnas sgo phyes /
bkra shis lhun po'i paN chen du bzhugs yod pa'i skabs /
sne gdong dpon sa ngag dbang bkra shis grags pa dang lha rgya ri ba mchod yon /
'bras spungs spyi so sogs kyis yang dang yang du gdan 'dren zhus stabs /
me glang lor bkra shis lhun po'i paN chen bsko gzhag gnang ste /
'bras spungs su phebs nas /
'bras spungs kyi chos khrir bzhugs /
'bras spungs su bla brang dga' ldan pho brang bzhengs /
rgyal dbang lnga bas bod yongs la dbang bsgyur pa nas gzhung sa dga' ldan pho brang phyogs las rnam rgyal zhes pa'ang /
pho brang 'di'i mtshan srid gzhung gi mtshan du gyur 'dug me byi lo nas rin spungs pa'i mnga' thang rim gyis nyams te /
sa stag lo nas rje 'di'i 'phrin las la brten /
se 'bras kyi dge 'dun pa rnams lha ldan smon lam chen mor 'tshogs chog pa byung /
me bya lor rje dge 'dun rgya mtsho 'phrin las shin tu rgyas /
'on kyang chos 'khor rgyal du bzhugs skabs 'bri gung bas chos lugs 'then 'khyer gyis /
'ol kha ba'i steng du dpung rgol byas te rdzing phyi shor /
'od sna sogs dge lugs pa'i dgon pa bco brgyad 'bri gung bas phrogs /
rgyal ba dge 'dun rgya mtsho dgung lo drug cu re lnga'i thog rab byung dgu ba'i chu stag lor 'das /
rgyal dbang sku phreng gsum pa bsod nams rgya mtsho /
rab byung dgu ba'i chu yos lor stod lung mdar sku bltams /
gdan sar bkod nas paN chen bsod nams grags pa sogs bsten te /
gsan bsam rgya chen po gnang stabs kun gyis gtsug tu bkur /
sde gzar khag la chings 'dum dang bka' khra sogs mdzad /
me 'brug lor yar lung sne gdong ba dang /
'phyongs rgyas nang so ma mthun par sde gzar chen po langs skabs /
rje 'di ba bar 'dum mdzad par phebs te zhi 'jags mdzad /
sa lug lor sne gdong gong ma chen po ngag dbang bkra shis grags pas rje bsod nams rgya mtshor kwan ding ta'i gu shrI hwong hang gi mtshan dang /
phyag dam dmar bo gnang chog pa'i bka' shog gnang ste /
sne gdong pho brang du gdan drangs nas chos 'brel rgya chen po zhus /
de'i phyi lor sne gdong gi zhal ngo rnams nang zhig byung ste sde 'khrug byung skabs /
rje 'di ba bar 'dum du phebs nas g.yul 'thab bkag slar yang sde srid phag gru ba nang zhig gi sde 'khrug skyid shod phyogs nas langs par /
grub mtha' so so'i bla chen rnams bar 'dum du byon yang phan pa cher ma byung skabs /
rgyal ba bsod nams rgya mtsho gdan drangs /
khong gis chings mdzad nas bka' khras bcad de dmag rnams so sor gyes /
chu khyi lor lha sar chu nyen chen po byung skabs chu rags gsar rgyag dang /
de nas bzung smon lam chen mo'i rjes thogs dge 'dun rnams kyis rags rdo skyel ba'i srol bzang btsugs /
sa sbrul lor bkra shis lhun por phebs /
gnas rnying ba chos kyi rgyal mtshan bkra shis lhun po'i paN chen du bsko gzhag mdzad /
gtsang phyogs kyi gnas chen rnams su phebs /
'brong rtser rgyal byed tshal du 'brug pa pad ma dkar bo dang mjal 'phrad gnang /
thugs snang gcig tu 'dres /
de nas bzung dge 'brug gnyis kyi mthun lam legs po byung /
shing phag lor rin spungs pas dmag khri phrag yas mas btegs nas /
stod lung sgal bo na khar phab /
sgal byang smon gsum bcom /
rim gyis skyid shod lha sar 'ong rtsis byas skabs /
rgyal dbang 'di bas drag po'i las sbyor mdzad pas phyir bzlog zer /
sog po cha har al than rgyal bos gdan 'dren yang yang zhus pas rjes ma'i skabs phebs rgyu'i zhal bzhes thog rab byung bcu ba'i me glang lo'i hor zla bcu gcig pa'i tshes nyer drug nyin /
'bras spungs nas chibs kha bsgyur /
de nas rim gyis phebs pas /
rma chen sbom ra'i gangs kyi nye 'dabs su slebs skabs /
al than rgyal bo'i phebs bsu dang bo ba ku tha'i ji sogs kyis gtso byas pa'i rta ba brgyad brgya 'byor /
a rigs dkar bo'i thang du se chen hong tha'i ji sogs phebs bsu gnyis pa rta ba stong gsum tsam 'byor /
de rjes nyin gsum gyi ring jo rigs thu tha'i ji sogs phebs bsu gsum pa rta ba sum brgya skor dang /
slar yang chos rje brtson 'grus bzang bo dang lo tsA ba gu shrI pak+Shi sogs kyis gtsos rta ba lnga brgya skor phebs bsur 'byor /
rab phyogs sa stag lo'i hor zla lnga ba'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin mtsho sngon gyi lho nub zad mtshams chab cha zhes pa'i sa char al than rgyal bo yab yum 'khor khri phrag dang bcas phebs bsur slebs nas /
dad gus chen pos bsdus te /
mchod yon thog mar mjal /
sa der sa 'dul mdzad de theg chen chos 'khor gling zhes pa'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs /
rgyal bos 'bul ba rgya chen po phul /
da nas sog yul du dam pa'i chos rgya chen po spel /
sngar mi shi ba'i rjes su shi bor dmigs nas /
srog gcod pa'i srol ngan yod /
mchod yon gros thog nas srol ngan de mtshams bcad /
gal te mi bsad pa byung na lus srol la khrims gcod /
rta phyugs bsad pa la nor thams cad 'phrog pa'i khrims bsgrags /
sngar ong bkod ces zer ba gshin po thams cad kyi gzugs byas te /
zla ba re re bzhin nya stong tshes brgyad gsum la phyugs bsad de khrag mchod byed /
lo dus kyi mchod pa la dbul phyug gi dbye bas phyugs shin tu mang bo bsad de mchod pa byed pa'i srol ngan de'i rgyun bcad /
ong bkod ces pa'i rten brten pa me la bsregs /
de'i tshab tu ye shes kyi mgon po phyag drug pa'i sku re 'jog pa dang /
de yang dkar mchod byed pa las khrag mchod byed mi chog pa'i khrims bkod /
rgya bod hor sog gi mi su la'ang 'phrog bcom byed mi chog pa'i khrims bcas /
mdor na dge ba bcu la gnas dgos pa'i khrims mang du bsgrags /
dbang rjes gnang sogs chos kyi char ba phab bo / /
rgyal dbang lnga ba'i rang rnam du kU la'i gos bzang gi rgyal ba bsod nams rgya mtsho'i rnam thar thad las /
lha sras mu ne dang 'khrungs rgyud gcig pa /
gnam sa'i dbang phyug al than chos kyi rgyal bo'i dbu blar gyur te sa'i tshangs pa de nyid kyis mi rigs mi gcig pa du ma'i dbus su /
gser las grub pa'i dbu rgyan /
bum pa /
rigs lnga'i phyag mtshan /
gser srang brgya las grub pa'i 'brug sder mo lngas mtshan pa /
kha ris la rdo rje 'chang tA la'i bla ma'i tham ga rgyal /
zhes hor yig gser du yod pa /
yo byad 'gangs che tshad med dang bcas /
tA la'i bla ma badzra d+ha ra zhes khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang gi las ka phul /
rgyal bo la'ang lha'i tshangs pa chen po /
zhes mtshan gnang zhing /
rgya nag gong ma lban li rgyal bos /
rgyal khams thams cad kyi bla ma gyig ching shri'i mtshan dang /
tham ga lung /
las zhwa /
las gos /
'ja' sa sogs kyi sngon du rgyal bo'i che ba'i rol mo sna tshogs dang bcas rgya nag gi mi dpon gsum gyis gtso byas te mi sna 'byor /
lu hang gsar ma'i na bza' cha tshang sogs dang /
gser dngul gos dar sogs pho brang gi dpyad pa mang du phul /
nged rang gi 'bangs su gyur pa'i sog po tsho chen bzhi bcu dang /
kan cu thang gi mi dpon sogs kyi re ba yongs su bskang ba legs shing /
pho brang chen por yang rim gyis gdan 'dren zhes pa sogs kyi bka' shog gnang zhes gsungs so / /
dus de nas bzung rgyal dbang sku phreng rim byon la tA la'i bla ma zhes yongs su grangs /
tA la ni sog po'i skad la rgya mtsho zer zhing /
rgya mtsho'i bla ma zhes pa'i go don ni /
thugs rje dang byin rlabs /
mtshan snyan dang 'phrin las sogs /
rgya mtsho chen po ltar mtha' dang mu med par rgya chen ba'i don yin par gsungs /
rgyal rigs gsum gyis gtso byas pa'i sog pa brgya phrag mang bo rab tu byung /
'ur bsdus kyi rgyal bos gdan drangs /
der phun tshogs gzhan phan sde zhes pa'i dgon pa btab /
yul du mar phebs /
chos lan mang bor gnang /
cha har rnams kyis rgya'i lcags ri'i nang khongs kyi sde la gnod 'tshe che bas /
rje 'di bas sog po rnams la chos dang 'brel ba'i bka' slob gnang nas bzung rgya'i rigs rnams la gnod 'tshe mi byed par gyur /
sa yos lor 'ur bsdus dang /
o rdo nang 'khrug pa 'dum mdzad de bde bar bkod /
mchod yon bka' gros thog nas bod sog 'brel ba byed mi sog phyogs nas dpon po kho lo che ching pA thur 'khor bcas mtsho khar 'jog rgyu dang /
bod phyogs nas sku tshab stong skor yon tan rgya tsho'i bsko gzhag byas te sog yul du rdzong dba' mdzad /
sne gdong gong mar lo ltar mtsho kha'i phyogs nas rta khral 'bul rgyu'i rgyun btsungs /
lcags 'brug lor khams stod li thang du phebs /
li thang dgon chen thub bstan byams chen phyogs thams cad las rnam par rgyal ba'i sde btab /
lcags sbrul lor rmar khams /
brag g.yab /
chab mdo sogs su phebs /
ldan chos 'khor dgon du phebs skabs al than rgyal bo'i sras du ring rgyal bo mi sna mang bo dang bcas /
al than rgyal bo gshegs pa'i bsngo zhu dang /
gdan 'dren du byon pa ltar mtsho khar chibs bsgyur /
chu lug lo'i lo sar skabs sku 'bum du phyag phebs /
der bshad grwa btsugs /
tsong kha'i phyogs su rgya dang hor 'khrug pa chen po yod par 'dum mdzad de kun bde skyid kyi lam du bkod /
de nas 'ur bsdus dpon se chen hong tha'i ji'i sde thog tu 'byor /
der dge 'dun gyi sde btsugs /
rab tu byung ba stong phra brgal ba byung /
shing bya lor se chen da'i ching gi sde thog tu phebs te /
phun tshogs dar rgyas gling gi dgon pa btab /
me khyi lor al than rgyal bo'i sras du ring gi gdan 'dren 'byor ba ltar /
chibs bsgyur gnang ste al than rgyal bo'i rgyal sa /
mkhar sngon por phebs /
mang tshogs la dbang bskur byin rlabs sogs gnang ba dang /
al than rgyal bo'i gdung zhugs la phul /
bsngo smon mdzad /
du ring khAng gi mchod yul du lo gcig tsam bzhugs /
du ring khAng yang glo bur du gshegs /
rje 'di bas yang snyung tshul cung zad bzhes /
sa byi lo'i hor zla dang bo'i zla mjug tu bro 'tshal ba'i tshul mdzad yod thog rgya nag gong ma'i gdan 'dren mi sna 'byor /
rten 'brel la dgongs phebs rgyu'i zhal bzhes gnang /
zla gsum pa'i tshes nyer bdun nyin sku 'das /
dgung grangs zhe drug pa yin 'dra /
gdung zhugs la phul nas gdung rus rnams zhabs 'bring ba rnams kyis 'bras spungs su gdan drangs so / /
rgyal dbang sku phreng bzhi ba yon tan rgya mtsho /
sog yul du yab thu med tha'i ji dang yum bA khen sbur gyi sras su rab byung bcu ba'i sa glang lo'i zla tshes nyin 'khrungs /
rgyal ba bsod nams rgya mtsho'i yang sprul du ngos bzung /
dgung lo gnyis bzhes skabs sog po'i dpon rigs dang /
sbyin bdag rnams kyis mkhar sngon por gdan drangs /
dga' ldan khri zur rgyal khang rtse ba dpal 'byor rgya mtshos thams cad mkhyen pa yon tan rgya mtsho zhes pa'i mtshan stsal /
dgung lo bcu bzhi'i thog lcags glang lor dpal ldan 'bras spungs dga' ldan pho brang gi khrir 'khod /
de rjes dga' ldan khri zur sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mkhan po mdzad de rab tu byung nas dge tshul gyi sdom pa bzhes /
bkra shis lhun po'i gdan sa paN chen bco lnga ba blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan dpal bzang bo rgyal dbang mchog gis gtsug gi cod pan du bsten te mdo sngags kyi chos bka' mang du gsan /
gong du bshad pa ltar bkra shis lhun por paN chen dge 'dun grub kyi gdan sar bzhugs mkhan rnams la paN chen zhes pa'i mtshan thogs la /
paN chen bco lnga ba blo bzang chos rgyan sku tshe gang la paN chen du bzhugs stabs /
de nas bzung paN chen blo bzang chos rgyan gyi sku phreng rnams la paN chen rin po che zhes mtshan de rgyun 'jags su byung /
shing 'brug lor rje 'di'i bka' gnang ltar 'on rgyal sras don yod chos kyi rgya mtshos mdo smad a mdo'i yul du dgon lung btab /
me lug lor bkra shis lhun por phebs /
slob dpon paN chen rin po che blo bzang chos rgyan la brgya 'bul dang bcas zla ba phyed gnyis lhag la chos bka' mang du zhus /
de skabs zhing shag pa tshe brtan rdo rje'i bu sde ba karma bstan srung dbang bos gtsang phyogs la dbang bsgyur pa'i skabs yin la /
de dang phyogs lhung can 'ga' zhig gis mi gus pa'i rnam 'gyur byas par grags /

se chen tha'i jis gtso byas pa'i sog 'grul dang /

skyid shod sde ba bsod nams rnam rgyal dang /
'dan pa 'tsho byed sogs kyis gtsang rgol gyi dus zing bslangs par /

gtsang rgyal gyi sras rnams gzhon nu nas gshegs /
gtsang rgyal khrir 'khod dag kyang dar ma dar thog nas 'das stabs /
gtsang rgyal khros nas /

de ltar byas mod /
phyis su mig sogs dbang bo gsar ba skyes te /
ri phug ces pa'i khong gi gdan sa nas bka' lung dkon po mang bo gnang ba dang mu mthud nas drag po'i las sbyor mdzad stabs /
de rjes lo gsum tsam las ma 'gro bar gu shrI bstan 'dzin gyis gtsang srid lhag med du bcom ste /
gtsang srid ming tsam lhag mar ma lus pa rje 'di ba'i mthu nus yin zhes rje 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i gsung gi 'jigs byed chos 'byung sogs rnam thar lo rgyus mang bo'i nang du 'dug go / /
lcags phag lor rje 'dis paN chen rin po che blo bzang chos rgyan 'bras spungs su spyan drangs te rdo rje phreng ba sogs dbang bka' rgya chen po gsan /
lo 'dir gtsang dmag gtos chen po yar rgyab pa'i thog tu 'ongs nas /
yar rgyab pa'i dbang cha tshang ma phrogs /
sku skal byin nas sa gzhan du phud /
shing stag lor rgyal dbang rin po ches paN chen rin po che'i drung las bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom pa bzhes /

lo der gtsang sde srid phun tshogs rnam rgyal gyis karma ba yab sras gzhis ka bsam 'grub rtser gdan drangs /

ser sbrengs zhu bar 'dzom dgos pa'i bka' phab /
lo der rgyal ba yon tan rgya mtsho dgung grangs nyer brgyad du slebs /

rgyal dbang sku phreng lnga ba blo bzang rgya mtsho /

yum khri lcam kun dga' lha mdzes kyi sras su 'khrungs /

sa rta lo'i zla ba bdun pa'i nang /

thu med tha'i ji'i sras lha btsun bgres gzhon gnyis dang /

khun du lung cho khur sogs hal ha'i rgyal rgyud /

gtsang srid phyogs nas ma nyan par mthar sog dmag dang /

da'i ching gis dmag sna drangs te /

byang stag lung sogs su bros /

chos rje stag lung bas chings mol zhus te /
se 'bras kyi grwa ba rnams sngar rgyun bzhin grwa sar bzhugs chog par byas kyang /
'bras spungs la gser zho nyis brgya'i chad pa dang /
se ra la gser zho brgya tham pa'i chad pa bzhag se 'bras la gser ster rgyu med pas dga' ldan pho brang ba'i zhal ngo bsod nams chos 'phel gyis rgyal du mdzod cig yod pa las gser len dgos tshul brjod de /

de rjes gtsang bas yar lung sogs kyi sde dpon rnams la ches mi 'tsham pa sha stag byas pa dang /

zug po nas la rtsis sprad /

gzim khang sde ba sna dkar rtse bas gtsang la yar zhus dang khag theg gnang stabs /
yum sras gnyis ka sna dkar rtser bzhugs chog pa byung /

lcags bya /
lor lha btsun blo bzang bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho dang /
gu ru hong tha'i jis gtsos hor sog gi dmag stong gnyis lha sar slebs /

zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bcu'i nyin /
glo bur du sog dmag gtsang ba'i dmag sgar thog tu brgyugs pas mi brgya phrag du ma bsad /

mda'i char 'bebs pa'i skabs su phebs /

se 'bras mchod gzhis rnams tshur sprad /

'phyongs rgyas sprul skur bab /

a mi sger ru bcom /

don 'khyol byung stabs /

rgyu mtshan zhus /
sog po'i rgyal blon rnams kyis gros bsdur byed skabs /

sog por skrag nas ngo ma bstan /

kar gtsang la 'brel lam ma byung /

de rjes 'dam gzhung brgyud nas phyir log de rjes zhwa dmar rab 'byams pa zer ba dang /

mi mngags nas rang gi bu ar sa lang dang /
de'i blon po gnyis bsad /

lha sa'i jo bo dang /

kar dge /

mgron gnyer bon gong ba /
rta nag 'o rlon pa /

tA ming rgyal bo'i rgyal sa phrags nas /

man /

dal gel dge slong dang /

yang no mon han ngag dbang lhun 'grub dar rgyas sam /
ming gzhan lha btsun ngag dbang rdo rjes mdzad pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags rgya mtsho'i rnam thar lha'i tam+bu ra'i rgyud kyi sgra dbyangs /
zhes bya ba las /
sog po shi ma thag pa'i ro nyos te drang don la mya ngan las 'das tshul tsam las nges don la gcig pur bros te a rigs 'grul ba dang bsdebs nas sog yul du bzhugs shing /
zhes sogs dang /
mdo smad a mdo'i yul du gser khog dang dzag rung sogs su gdan sa mdzad cing /
'gro don rgya chen po bskyangs mthar sog yul a lag sha ru sa lug lor sku gshegs zhes dgung grangs lnga bcu nga drug la gshegs pa sogs bshad 'dug rnam thar rtsom pa bo a lag sha wang gi sras red /
rnam thar 'di la 'ga' zhig gis tshangs dbyangs pa'i gsang ba'i rnam thar zer /
deng sang 'di pe cin nas lcags par btab yod /
'ga' zhig gis lo rgyus snga ma nges don yin /
phyi ma ni tshangs dbyangs pa rdzus ma red zer /
yang la las snga ma drang don dang phyi ma nges don yin zer /
chab srid skor 'di snyog dra che bas /
ngo ma gang yin sus shes /
tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho rgya nag tu gdan drangs pa'i lo der /
ngag dbang ye shes rgya mtsho rgyal ba'i sprul skur ngos bzung ste /
po ta lar gdan drangs /
de yang ye shes rgya mtsho 'di ni /
rab byung bcu gcig pa'i drug cu ba me stag la tshangs dbyangs pa dgung lo bzhi ba'i skabs su bar khams tsha rong kha ba dkar bor 'khrungs /
sku na phra dus lcags po ri la bzhugs /
dgung lo bcu bzhi ba sa yos la 'bras spungs su phebs nas slob gnyer gnang /
sle lung rje drung blo bzang 'phrin las kyi drung nas bsnyen par rdzogs /
mtshan la rin po che ye shes rgya mtsho gsol /
gar phebs la tshul khrims kyi dri ngad rgyang ring bor khyab pas 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po zhig yin par cha 'jog byed pa red zer /
dgung grangs nyer gnyis pa'i me phag lor po ta la'i khrir 'khod /
zla nang paN chen rin po che gdan 'dren zhus te /
tshes nyin lha ldan gtsug lag khang gi jo bo rin po che'i mdun du rgyal ba pad dkar 'dzin pa la dge tshul dang /
bsnyen rdzogs chabs cig tu gnang ste /
mtshan ngag dbang ye shes rgya mtsho zhes stsal /
yongs grags la rgyal ba pad dkar 'dzin pa zhes zhu ba de 'di ba red /
rje 'di'i dgung lo so gnyis pa me bya lor o rod jun gar gyi tha'i ji dga' ldan tshe ring don 'grub kyis jun gar gyi dmag mang bo khrid de bod yul du slebs nas lha bzang bsad /
me bya lo 'di nas lo bzhi ba lcags byi lor rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho gdan drangs /
pad dkar 'dzin pa ngag dbang ye shes rgya mtsho bod nas zhe hor du spyan drangs /
zhe hor du /
lha khang ljang gu zhes pa bsam yas la dpe blangs nas bzhengs pa dang /
po ta la'i pho brang zhig kyang bzhengs nas /
der bzhugs su bcug sogs yul nas grwa ba stong gnyis tsam bsdus nas mtshan nyid kyang btsugs /
sog po rnams kyis khong la zhe hor tA la'i bla ma zer zhing /
ching gong mas mkhan po ho thog thu ngag dbang ye shes /
zhes zhu ba 'dra /
rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho dgung lo bcu dgu bzhes pa me rta lo'i rnam thar du /
mkhan po ho thog thu ngag dbang ye shes rgya mtsho sku gshegs pa'i bsngo zhus byung ba la dgongs rdzogs kyi dge ba rnams byang chub tu bsngo bar mdzad /
ces pa de /
zhe hor du bzhugs pa'i rgyal dbang de nyid yin na /
dgung lo zhe gcig pa'i skabs su gshegs pa 'dra'o / /
zhes cha har dge bshes kyi gsung bde legs 'byung gnas las gsungs /
zhe hor ? la deng sang khrin te ? zer gyin 'dug der bkra shis lhun po dang /
bde mchog lha khang sogs lha khang mang bo 'dug bdag kyang lor de gar song nas bdun gcig la bsdad /
bde legs 'byung gnas las /
"rje ngag dbang ye shes rgya mtsho ni /
rgyal bo lha bzang gis rje 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i drung du gsung brtag zhus nas ngos 'dzin mdzad /
ces zer ba sogs kyi gtam rgyun yod /
de bden na ye shes rgya mtsho de nyid rgyal dbang rin po che'i sprul ba gcig gam /
ji ltar sprul ba yin pa ngos bzung mdzad pas dgos pa chen po yod par nges shing /
rje de nyid rgyun gyi thugs dam nyams bzhes sogs gzhan dang mi 'dra ba /
gang zag khyad par can zhig yin zhing /
tshul khrims kyi dri ngad rgyang ring bor bro ba yin /
zhes de dus kyi zhabs phyi sogs nas thos pa'i gtam yod par 'dug go / /
'di las zhe hor gyi tA la'i bla ma zhes phyogs 'dir grags shing /
'di bzhugs pa'i lha khang ljang gu zhes pa deng sang yang zhe hor na yod do / /
" zhes gsungs /
tshangs dbyangs pa rgya khrid skabs su la mo tshangs pa'i sku rten gyis /
tshangs dbyangs rgya mtsho rgyal ba'i sprul sku min par gsungs pa dang /
sprul sku gzhan zhig yod ces lung bstan pa red zer srol yod /
lung bstan de yongs rdzogs ma mthong la /
mgo'i tshig rkang gnyis mthong ba ni /
phyi mun nang du ye shes sgron me 'bar /
nga ni gong ma dbyer med du 'dun pa byed /
ces 'dug de ni phyi mun nag ste mi dkyus ma'i nang du /
ye shes rgya mtsho bzhugs yod pa /
gong ma lnga ba chen mo dang dbyer med yin /
zhes pa e yin snyam pa dang /
de rjes da lta gzhung gi gnas s yod pa las /
lha dang mkha' 'gros btsal kyang rnyid par dka' /
zhes gsungs pa de /
da lta gzhung dga' ldan pho brang gi gnas 'bras spungs su yod pa las sbas pa'i tshul grwa rkyang dkyus ma'i lugs su yod stabs sus kyang mi shes /
zhes pa'i don du go ba yin snyam /
rgyal bo lha bzang bas lo bcu gnyis yas mas la dbang bsgyur /
se ra'i tshogs chen 'du khang chen mo gsar bzhengs dang byams sku chen mo bzhengs /
'du khang rnying ba'i nang du 'dam du yod pa'i gu shrI bstan 'dzin gyi ur ge grwa tshang spos te sngags pa grwa tshang btsugs /
blon 'khor gtso bo ni da'i ching pA thur bsod nams mgon po /
drung yig pa pho lha bsod nams stobs rgyal /
'bum thang ba sogs shin tu mang /
rgyal bo 'di'i dus /
hor sbra nag khag bzhi'i 'brog rigs rnams kyis /
bod gzhung la lo dus kyi dpya khral ma phul bar brten /
drung chen pho lha dang /
lha rtse skyid spug pa dpung bcas song nas mtha' bskor te /
lo thang 'bul rgyu dus las mi yol bar bya rgyu byas /
tha'i ji la rta bzang lnga bcu tham pa'i chad pa bcad /
de tsam las jun gar gyi btsan 'dzul yong ba'i bar du nang 'khrug byung ba'i lo rgyus mthong rgyu mi 'dug go / /
lha bzang ba dang /
jun gar tshe dbang rab brtan ni sngar mthun yang /
phyis mi mthun pa'i rkyen ni 'ga' zhig gis /
de'i skabs jun gar dang /
man ching gong ma gnyis kyis dmag 'khrug yang yang byed skabs yin la /
lha bzang nas ching la ngo rgol gyi shed ma thon pas /
sngon la dbus gtsang blangs te /
de nas mtsho sngon phyogs nas ching gong ma la dpung 'jug byed bsam pa red zer /
la las zer ba ni /
lha bzang gi bu che ba dga' ldan bstan 'dzin jun gar gyi mag par 'gro skabs sgam gyi nang du byad 'khor bcug pa dang /
rim gro ba'i tshul du byad ma kha shas kyang mngags pa tshor nas dmag btang ba red zer /
gang ltar rgya nag tu khang shi nga drug pa me bya lo'i zla bdun pa'i nang jun gar dmag 'dam du 'byor /
zla tshes nyin /
bod dmag gis jun gar gyi dmag sgar thog dpung 'jug byas kyang /
nyam nyes chen po byung /
de nas jun gar bas bod kyi dmag dang dmangs mi rnams la /
nged cag bod la dmag rgyag par yong ba min /
bod kyi spyi don dang /
rgyal dbang gi sku don la yong ba yin sogs mgo skor gyi gtam sna tshogs lab pas /
bod 'bangs rnams phar rgol byed pa'i shugs nyams te /
de nas jun gar gyi dmag lha sa'i phyogs su bskyod nas /
bod kyi sa srung rnams kyis 'gog ma thub par /
ra mo che'i phyogs nas lha sa'i nang du 'dzul /
lha bzang gi sras chung ba sur ya g.yog gnyis bcas mtsho sngon phyogs su 'bros bcug lha bzang 'khor nyung shas bcas pho brang po ta la'i nang du 'dzul nas sgo gtan /
zla tshes nyin lha bzang dang blo bzang chos 'phel dpon g.yog gnyis /
rtse zhol gzhung sgo nas bud de rta bzhon nas jun gar ba'i dmag sgar thog brgyugs nas jun gar ba kha shas bsad /
kha shas rmas pa'i mthar dmag mang bos bskor te dpon g.yog gnyis ka bsad /
de rjes pad dkar 'dzin pa khri las phab bo / /
de ltar rgyal bo lha bzang bas lo ngo bcu gnyis la bod khams yongs la dbang bsgyur to / /
rab nyi me bya lo'i zla tshes nyin gdugs dkar ja'i sang gis dmag brgya skor khrid de /
po ta ltar song nas rnam rgyal grwa tshang gtor /
tshes nyin rdor brag dang /
smin gling gi zhal ngo rnams dang /
rgyal bo lha bzang ba'i dus kyi mi drag rnams btson du bcug zla de'i tshes nyin /
tshe ring don 'grub /
gdugs dkar chos 'phel te /
ja'i sang gsum gyis /
bla brang steng du dbus gtsang gi bla dpon rnams bsdus te /
rnying lugs gtan nas byed mi chog rnying ma'i sku gsung thugs rten rnams 'dor dgos /
zhes bsgrags /
de nub smin gling lo chen dang /
blo bzang bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan /
gdung sras 'gyur med rgya mtsho sogs rnying ma'i bla chen khag gcig skyid chu'i 'gram du khrid de bkrongs /
de nas yang smin gling gdung sras gzhon pa dang /
phyag mdzod zhabs drung legs grub /
gzhung zhabs gtso che ba /
dngos gzhi ba /
pad ma tshe ring /
rgyal rtse lcang lo can /
chang khyim pa /
gnya' nang lcags ra spug pa sogs mang bo bsad /
rdo rje brag smin grol gling /
chu shur thar ba gling /
gsang sngags byang chub gling sogs rnying dgon rnams bshigs so / /
de dus jun gar gyi dpon rnams kyis gros thog nas stag rtse ba lha rgyal rab brtan bod kyi srid 'dzin dpon du bskos /
pho lha ba bsod nams stobs rgyal yang lha bzang gi gser yig pa drung yig yin stabs /
'bras spungs su gab yod pa shes nas bzung /
srog chad gcod nye'i skabs /
sde srid stag rtse ba dang /
sog po jun gar ba 'bras spungs sgo mang mkhan po ngag dbang phun tshogs gnyis kyis ngo chen zhus te btson grol btang /
de ltar jun gar gyis me bya lo'i zla pa nas bzung /
lcags byi lo'i lo mjug bar du lo ngo gsum tsam la dbus gtsang yongs rdzogs bzung na yang mdo smad du shugs ma slebs 'dug go / /
rgyal dbang sku phreng bdun pa bskal bzang rgya mtsho /
rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho ni /
khams li thang byams pa gling gi zhol gyi grong sde'i nang du sa byi lo'i zla tshes nyin sku bltams /
gnas chung chos skyong sku rten gyis tshangs dbyangs pa'i sprul skur ngos bzung /
shing rta lo dgung grangs bdun thog sde dge rdzong gsar dang lcang ra dgon sogs su phebs skabs sde dge dpon bstan pa tshe ring gis kyang sne len gzab rgyas zhus /
de rjes mtsho sngon gyi ching wang pA thur tha'i ji dang /
dpon ching wang 'ju nang /
blo bzang bstan skyong rab brtan /
ngag dbang chos 'phel sogs kyis thos te gdan zhu'i mi sna btang ste /
shing rta lo der ching wang dga' ldan er te ni 'ju nang gi urger gdan drangs /
'ju nang gis 'bad brtson gyis ching gong mar zhus pa sogs la brten /
ching gong mas kyang mi sna mngags te /
sog bod kyi dpon chen rnams kyis sku 'bum du gdan drangs /
sa phag lor gong ma khang shi'i rgyal sras bcu bzhi ba sku 'bum du yang srid bskal bzang rgya mtsho'i mdun du bcar ba dang /
bstan 'dzin ching wang dang /
dga' ldan 'ju nang gis gtso byas dpon rnams kyis sku 'bum nas yang srid rin po che dbus phyogs su gdan 'dren zhu rgyu'i gros 'chams byung nas gong mar zhus te gong mas kyang rgyal dbang lnga ba'i sprul sku yin par khas blangs nas /
sku phreng drug pa yin pa'i 'ja' sa dang /
gser gyi glegs bu tham ga bcas stsal ba sogs rnam thar du gsal /

de skabs o rod jun gar phyogs su /
o rod dang ching gong ma'i dmag gis dmag 'khrug byed pa dang /
mdo smad nas rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho bod sog rgya gsum gyi dmag 'bor chen bcas 'byon gyin yod pa sogs 'ur sgra dbus phyogs su khyab pas dbus dpon kha shas kyis jun gar la ngo log byas pa sogs la brten /
jun gar gyi dmag rnams 'dug ma bzod par rang yul du bros so / /

pho brang po ta la'i sku gong ma dag gi khrir zhabs sor 'khod /

lcam /
sras chung ba bcas rgya yul du khyer /
lcags glang lo'i lo sar skabs /
stod sgar dpon khang chen nas bsod nams rgyal bor /
da'i ching pA thur gyi cho lo byin /
thab rten du 'tsho rten yar 'brog gling gi 'dzin dbang stsal /
bod rgya sog gsum gyi mi bdun mnyam 'brel lhan tshogs phyir bsdus /
da'i ching pA thur khang chen nas la /
srid rogs blon lta bur pe se nga phod pa /
lum pa ba /
sbyar ra ba /
pho lha ba bcas mi lnga lhan 'brel gyi srid gzhung btsugs /
bod ljongs su dbang bsgyur /
po ta la'i zhol du de dus btsugs pa'i rdo ring yod /
man ching gong ma'i sku tshab la da'i si cang jun dang /
tA la'i bla ma'i sku srung lta bur cang jun tshe dbang nor bu /
dmag bzhi stong bcas lha sar bzhag ste /
phebs skyel du bcar ba'i rgya sog gi dpon rigs 'khor bcas phyir log pa red /

bod kyi dpon rigs rnams mdun gral dang /

don smin ma byung ba dang /
sngar bod du gu shrI han bstan 'dzin chos rgyal gyi gdung rgyud cig bod kyi rgyal bor bsko ba'i srol yod mod /

rab nyi chu yos lo nas mtsho sngon bstan 'dzin wang sogs kyis man ching gong mar ngo rgol byed pa'i 'khrug zing bslangs pa dang /

shing 'brug lo ching gong ma g.yung Ting khri lo dang bor lha sdod a sa am ban dang rgya dmag tshang ma phyir 'then byas /
mtsho sngon phyogs mdo smad byang rgyud du /
bod sog gis ching gong ma la ngo log byed pa'i zing 'khrug chen po langs /
rgya dpon 'ga' gsod rmas dang /
rgya mkhar kha shas gtor bshigs sogs ngo rgol rgya mi chung ba tsam byung /
der brten rgya dmag chu brdol ba bzhin byung ste /
bod sog gi mi 'bum phrag mang bo bsad /
mi sde khri phrag mang bo brlags /

dgon lung /
