phyogs ris dang /
phyogs 'then byas te /
srid 'khyor ba'i lugs ngan khyab gdal du gyur /
pho lha bas nga lum sbyar gsum gyis byed ngan zhig byed 'ong snyam ste /
khang chen nas la srog byol du song na legs tshul bshad kyang snang rtog mi gtong bar bsdad /
pho lha rang nas lcam la nad byung bar khag bzhag nas dgongs zhus kyis gtsang phyogs su song ste rgyal rtser bsdad /
nga lum sbyar gsum gyis khang chen nas dang /
pho lha ba gnyis 'khor nye du dang bcas pa gsod rgyu'i gros byas te /
me lug lo'i zla tshes nyin lha sa'i gtsug lag khang gi gzim chung khams gsum nang du khang chen nas dang /
nga lu sbyar gsum tshogs 'du zhig 'tshogs /
yol ba'i phag tu gshed ma sbas yod pa des glo bur du khang nas pa'i skra nas 'jus shing nga lum sbyar gsum gyis gri phyung ste lag rub kyis bsad /
sgo na yod pa'i khang nas pa'i srung dmag rnams gzhan gsum gyi dmag gis lag rub kyis bsad /
de'i phyi nyin gshed ma btang ste khang nas pa'i lcam gnyis ka bsad /
yang gshed ma btang ste /
nag chu mkhan po dang /
ja'i sang gnyis ka bsad /
de nas gshed ma bkra shis dpal rab sogs pho lha ba 'khor bcas gsod par gtsang du btang yang /
pho lha bar bya shor te /
sras gnyis dang 'khor kha shas bcas gtsang stod du song ste /
mda' dpon lcang lo can dang /
bsam 'grub gling ba gnyis la yi ge btang ste /
da'i ching pA thur khang nas pa'i dgra sha len phyir dbus phyogs su dmag bskyod dgos pa'i bka' bskul btang /
de bzhin spo rong gi dpon a jo dang /
mnga' ris kyi sgar dpon dga' bzhi ba sogs bskul te pho lha rang gi dmag bcas gtsang dmag 'bor chen gyis /
me lug lo'i zla tshes nyin dbus phyogs su dmag bskyod byas /
dbus phyogs nas nga lum sbyar gsum gyis dbus dmag stong phrag kha shas khrid gtong gis gtsang dmag la rgol 'gog byed du gtsang phyogs su lhags /
de'i tshe gtsang ngam ring gi dpon nu ma pas nga lum sbyar gsum la gsang yig bskur ba pho lha ba'i lag tu 'byor /
de ma thag dmag mngags nas ngam ring nas kho bzung ste /
rkang lag dang lus thams cad thag pas bcings nas /
g.yang gzar ngos nas rbab la bsgril te bsad /
de nas 'brong rtse dang 'bras khud rgyud du gtsang dbus kyi dmag gis g.yul 'gyed thengs kha shas byas kyang rgyal pham cher ma byung /
dbus dmag gis gtsang gi mi ser dang dgon sde 'ga' la 'phrog bcom gyis gyong rgud chen po byung zer /
slar yang lo de'i zla ba nas gtsang dbus kyi dmag 'khrugs te phan tshun gsod rmas chen po byung /
de skabs rgyal dbang rin po ches kyang bde 'jags kyi don gsung bka' nan mo bskur ba dang paN chen rin po che'i mgron gnyer sa khud pa dang /
sa skya bdag chen rin po che'i mgron gnyer ngag dbang sogs kyis re zhig dmag mtshams 'jog pa'i chings yig bzhag ste /
phan tshun gyis dmag mi bzung ba rnams glod bkrol btang /
sa sprel lor slar yang gtsang dmag dbus phyogs su bskyod de 'phan yul brgyud /
lum pa ba dpung bcas la 'thab bzhin dmag bskyod byas pas nga lum sbyar gsum gyi dmag pham ste /
po ta la'i nang du 'dzul nas rgyal dbang la skyabs zhus /
pho lha ba dpung bcas /
sa sbrel lo'i zla tshes nyin lha sar 'byor te dbus gtsang gi bdag por gyur /
rgyal dbang sogs bla ma rnams kyis ngo chen zhus par brten /
re zhig gung blon nga lum sbyar gsum rang shag tu srung dmag bzhag nas 'dug bcug pho lha bas man ching gong ma la zhu yig phul te /
don gcod kyi ra mdar bos /
de rjes man ching gong ma'i mi sna a li khan am ban dang /
me ring dzam gi sogs dmag 'bum phrag gcig dang bcas dbus su 'byor /
nga lum sbyar gsum khongs gtogs bcas btson du bcug nyin gcig mi drag zhan brgya phrag mang bo 'tshogs pa'i dbus su /
nga lum sbyar gsum /
skyor lung bla ma /
rnam rgyal grwa tshang gi gnyer ba /
nga lum sbyar gsum gyi gnyen nye du bu phrug sogs mi grangs bcu dgu dmar gsod byas /
bud med phru gu kha shas rgya yul du rgyang 'phud btang ngo / /
me tA rin dang /
seng tA rin zer ba'i am ban gnyis dmag stong gnyis dang bcas pa bsdad /
gzhan rnams phyir log rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho'i mdzad spyod bka' gdams gong ma nang bzhin gnang bas mi dmangs mtho dman skya ser tshang mas dad gus lhur blangs stabs /
pho lha ba phrag dog 'phar te /
rgyal dbang rin po cher /
lo rjes mar man ching gong ma rgya bod sa mtshams su lta skor la phebs rgyu yin pas /
khyed gong mar mjal 'phrad kyi don du khams la song zhes bka' phab /
sa sprel lo'i zla tshes nyin mdo khams su chibs kha bsgyur /
sa bya lo'i zla tshes nyin li thang du 'byor /
lcags sprel lo'i zla tshes nyin mgar thar phyogs su chibs kha bsgyur te /
mgar thar du dgon pa btab /
lo ngo mthong bdun tsam la mgar thar du bzhugs /
de'i ring la'ang khri ngag dbang mchog ldan yongs 'dzin du bsten nas slob gnyer dang mdo sngags kyi gsan pa rgya chen po mdzad /
de nas bod dbus lha ldan du phebs rgyu gtan khel te man ching gong ma'i rgyal sras bcu bdun pa dang /
lcang skya rin po che rol ba'i rdo rje dpon g.yog phebs rdzong du phebs /
rgyal sras kyis rgyal dbang la chos zhus rjes phyir log ho thog thu lcang skya rol ba'i rdo rjes phebs skyel zhus te /
shing yos lo'i zla tshes nyin mdo khams phyogs kyi dpon dmag skya ser rgya chen pos phebs skyel zhus te dbus phyogs su chibs bsgyur /
zla tshes nyin lha ldan gtsug lag khang du zhabs sor 'khod de /
mi dbang pho lha bas snar thang bka' 'gyur par brkos pa'i par phud kyis gtso byas pa'i 'bul chen btegs /
chu phag lor o rod jun gar gyi dpon dga' ldan tshe ring dbang bo'i mi sna sum brgya skor yong ste rgyal dbang rin po cher 'bul chen dang dbus gtsang gi rten khag la mchod 'bul byas /
shing byi lor sde dge'i dpon gyis bka' 'gyur par brkos pa'i par phud 'bul mkhan gyi mi sna 'byor ba la bsngags brjod dang /
gsol ras 'bor chen stsal /
shing byi lo der ching gong ma chen lung gis /
g.yung hwa kung du mtshan nyid grwa tshang /
rgyud pa grwa tshang /
rig gnas grwa tshang gsar 'dzugs par bla ma las sne bcas rdzong bda' mdzad /
lcags bya lo nas 'go btsugs te lcang skya rol ba'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i dag yig mkhas pa'i 'byung gnas kyi shing par phud /
rab byung bcu gsum pa'i me yos lo'i zla tshes nyin sde srid pho lha ba bsod nams stobs rgyal gnya' bar gnyan 'bur byung ba ma sos par tshe las 'das /
de ltar mi dbang pho lha ba bsod nams stobs rgyal gyis lo ngo mthong nyi shu tsam la dbang bsgyur /
rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho la rgya sog bod gsum sogs kyis dad 'dun che zhing gus 'dud lhur blangs par sde srid pho lha ba bsod nams stobs rgyal phrag dog rgyas nas dngos su log sgrub mang du byas pa dang /
lkog nas rgyal dbang dang lcang skya rnam gnyis la mthu byad byas pa'i lo rgyus yang snang ngo / /
lcang skya'i rnam thar du'ang gsal pho lha ba la sras gnyis yod /
che ba gung 'gyur med tshe brtan mnga' ris kyi spyi dpon du bskos /
chung ba 'gyur med rnam rgyal la da la'i da'i ching pA thur gyi cho lo dang bcas bod kyi rgyal bor bskos /
da'i ching pA thur 'gyur med rnam rgyal gyis lo bzhi tsam la srid dbang bzung /
kho'i spun che ba mnga' ris gung 'gyur med tshe brtan dang ma mthun par mnga' ris phyogs su dmag drangs /
mnga' ris kyi mi drag zhan mang bo bsun gtser gyis dus mi bde bar byas /
dga' ldan khri ba nam mkha' bzang la drag po'i las sbyor mdzad de mnga' ris gung bsgral dgos zhus kyang /
khong gis dga' ldan khri bas mi gsod mi thub gsungs pas kho ma dga' ba /
khri las phab ste rgyud pa dri med gser khrir bskos /
mthar mnga' ris gung lha sar bka' mol gnang bar yong skabs mi mngags te lam nas lkog gsod byas /
lcags rta lor /
smon lam chen mo'i skabs kho'i gcen mnga' ris gung gi dge rtsa yin zer nas rgyal dbang rin po che tshogs dbur gdan 'dren zhus nas bsngo smon zhu ba sogs byas /
gzhan yang mdo mkhar zhabs drung la /
khyed dang dpon slob byams pa rin po che sogs kyis mnga' ris gung la dmag bskul byed kyin 'dug ces pa sogs gzhi med gleng 'gel gyis 'dri gcod byas /
dbus gtsang gi dpung chen bskul nas byang phyogs kyi ri dwags yod dgu bsad /
gzhon nu pho mo rnams bsdus te glu len bro gar gyis dus 'da' bar byas pa sogs la brten nas drag zhan kun gyi yid bsun par byas /
de'i skabs mdo mkhar zhabs drung gi chibs rta la mda' brgyab par ma zad /
'khor gzhon nu zhig kyang don med du mda' brgyab ste bsad /
sa sbrul lor paN chen rin po che dpal ldan ye shes /
rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho'i mdun du bsnyen rdzogs zhu bar phebs te /
zla tshes nyin jo bo rin po che'i spyan sngar bsnyen par rdzogs /
yab sras gnyis ka'i thugs bzhed la gzhan yang bka' chos mang tsam gnang zhu'i re ba yod kyang /
srid skyong 'gyur med rnam rgyal 'dis g.yo thabs kyis bdun phrag gsum tsam las bzhugs ma bcug par phyir phebs dgos byung /
sa 'brug lor srid skyong 'gyur med rnam rgyal gyis /
bod du yod pa'i rgya dmag rnams kyis bod mi ser la brnyas gtse dang rgyu nor za rngam che bas /
man ching gi dpon dmag gcig kyang med par phyir 'then byed dgos zhes lha sdod kyi rgya dpon gnyis la yang yang zhus par brten /
gong ma chen lung gis bod sdod am ban gyi sku srung lta bur rgya dmag brgya tsam las 'phro ma tshang ma phyir 'then byed rgyu dang /
am ban ngo g.yog dang /
dmag 'phro ma bcas kyis /
bod mi ser la 'phrog bcom dang /
brdab gsig mi 'byung ched phogs thob dgos mkho 'dang nges gnang rgyu yin tshul khas len byas /
lcags rta lor da la'i pA thur 'gyur med rnam rgyal gyis slar yang /
ching gong ma la bod sdod am ban gnyis dang dmag 'phro ma gcig kyang ma lus par phyir 'then dgos zhes /
yi ge phul 'dug zer /
gzhan yang jun gar la mthun lam byed pa'i mi sna gtong yong byas pa'i gnas tshul am ban sogs kyis shes pa dang /
bod nang gi mi drag du ma zhig srid skyong la mi dga' ba sogs kyi rkyen las /
am ban gnyis kyis g.yo thabs kyis da la'i pA thur 'gyur med rnam rgyal g.yog gnyis bcas bsad /
'gyur med rnam rgyal gyi mgron gnyer blo bzang bkra shis sogs kyis dmag khrid de 'ongs nas /
am ban gnyis sogs rgya mi mthong tshad bsad /
tha na tshong ba /
za khang /
sprang bo sogs rgya mi mi grangs pho mo nyis brgya bzhi bcu lhag pho brang po ta lar skyabs zhur song ba dag la rgyal dbang dngos su phebs te srog skyob zhus par ma zad /
bka' shog kyang sbyar /
'on kyang bka' shog kyang gted /
yongs 'dzin khri chen ngag dbang mchog ldan phebs te srog skyob zhus kyang bka' brtsi rgyu phar zad /
blo bzang bkra shis sogs kyis khri rin po che la tshig ngan mang du brjod de /
po ta la'i ra ba'i nang du 'dzul ba'i rgya mi thams cad bsad de /
po ta la'i ra ba khrag gis dmar bor byas 'dug ces rnam thar lo rgyus kha shas su 'dug go / /
de rjes gong ma chen lung gis /
dga' bzhi rdo ring gung paN Di ta mgon po dngos grub rab brtan zer ba der gnas skabs su 'gan 'khur dgos shing /
blo bzang bkra shis sogs gte bo shor mi chog ces bka' phab /
mgron gnyer blo bzang bkra shis sogs jun gar phyogs su bros 'gro rgyu byed skabs /
gung paN Di tas de dag gang du slebs kyang 'dzin dgos zer ba'i bka' bsgrags pa ltar /
'dzin bzung byas te /
blo bzang bkra shis /
dpal grong shar ba /
srang sbug pa sogs mi mang po zhig la lha ldan lcang lo can gyi sgo ra'i nang du srog chad bcad /
da la'i pA thur 'gyur med rnam rgyal gyi sras dar rgyas tshe ring dang /
lcam chen chun sogs rgyang 'phud btang ngo / /
mi ring bar ching gong mas mngags pa'i a li am ban dang tsong thung tshe gung ye rnam rgyal am ban /
srung dmag lnga brgya dang bcas 'byor ro / /
de nas gong ma'i bka' lung dang rgya bod gros mthun gyis lcags lug lor rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtshor bod kyi chos srid gnyis ka'i dbang cha tshang ma phul /
'di'i sngon rgyal dbang lnga ba'i dus nas bzung /
rgyal bo sde srid logs su yod pas de dag gis srid bskyangs /
rgyal dbang rin po ches gtso cher chos kyi bya ba mdzad /
srid la dbang ba'i rgyal bo 'gyur med rnam rgyal gyi bar du yod mod /
'di nas bzung ste rgyal dbang nar ma son pa'i bar du rgyal bo'am srid skyong bsko gzhag dang /

bka' blon bzhi ni /

thon pa sri chod tshe brtan /
ser mo ba mgron gnyer dar han rnams bsko bzhag go / /

rgyal dbang rin po che la bod sog gi drag zhan ches mang bo dad 'dun shin tu che stabs /
de nas bzung bod kyi srid dbang 'phrog res kyis khyod gsod nga gsod kyi nang dme re zhig mtshams chad de /
mi ser byings bde 'jags sos dal ngang la gnas thub pa byung ngo / /
'di dag gi skor rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho'i rnam thar sogs su shin tu gsal lo / /
chu sprel lor paN chen dpal ldan ye shes dbus su phebs nas /
rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho'i zhal snga las bka' lung dbang khrid bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan /
shing khyi lo'i zla pa'i nang rtse slob grwa btsugs te slob dpon tshag sgur ba bskal bzang 'phrin las bsko gzhag mdzad /
rtse zhol du sku rten bris 'bur bzhengs pa'i bzo grwa gsar 'dzugs mdzad /
de ltar chos srid gnyis cha nas 'gran zla bral ba'i mdzad pa 'od dkar gyis nor 'dzin sgeg mo dkar chab tu btang /
me glang lo'i zla gnyis par dgung lo lnga bcu'i thog sku'i bkod pa bsdus so / /
khong gis sku tshe gang bor sdom gsum dag pa nyams len gyi mthil du bzung nas /
'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis dus 'da' bar mdzad /
dge sbyong gi chos bzhi dang du blangs nas /

chags sdang mgo snyom mdzad /

nang 'khrug sde gzar dang /
rgyal khab bar gyi 'khrug zing gang yang ma byung bas /
bu rta nor gsum brlag ma dgos shing dmangs byings kyis bde 'jags ngang 'tsho ba brgal thub pa byung ngo / /
khong 'das ma thag bka' blon rnams dang /
sku bcar khag gdan sa gsum gyi slob dpon /
drung yig ser skya sogs gros bsdur byas te /
gcig mthun spyi mos ltar /
de mo sprul sku ngag dbang 'jam dpal bde legs rgya mtshor no mon han gyi cho lo dang bcas rgyal tshab tu mnga' gsol /
bla sprul khongs nas rgyal tshab tu bzhugs mkhan thog ma khong yin zhes gsungs /

paN chen dpal ldan ye shes kyis /

bla ma chos rdzong ba dang /
rag shag dge rgan gnyis dge rgan du bskos /
'brug pa rnams slob gnyer ma thon bar du zur chas rgyun gtong dang /
sdod gnas bcas kyi sku drin bskyangs /
me phag lor mchod gzhis /
mi chen gzhis ka'i lam lugs /
phyi yong mi sna la sne len byed lugs /
lam yig ster lugs sogs gsar ba gtan la phab /
gong ma chen lung gis zhe hor po ta la dang /
bkra shis lhun po zhes pa'i chos sde gsar rgyag gnang ba'i mkhan po dang /
mkhas btsun bzang gsum 'dzom pa kha shas gtong dgos zhes zhus pa ltar /
sgo mang dge bshes srad rgyud mkhan po sangs rgyas 'od zer /
sgo mang mdung nag zhabs drung ngag dbang chos grags /
blo gling blo bzang chos grags /
dbu mdzad rgyud smad dge slong ngag dbang rin chen dang /
dge slong ngag dbang skal ldan bcas rdzong bda' mdzad /
lcags yos lor sngar rgya dang o rod 'khrug skabs /
bros byol gyis u ru si'i sa mtshams su bsdad pa'i jun gar ba rnams rang yul du yong chog pa dang gong ma'i rgya dmag gis gnod pa mi byed pa'i don la rgyal dbang mchog gis bka' drin yang dag pa stsal /
rgyal tshab de mo no mon han ngag dbang 'jam dpal bde legs rgya mtshos chab srid kyi thugs 'gan lo nyi shu rtsa gcig la gnang ste /
me bya lo'i zla tshes nyin bstan rgyas gling du sku gshegs /
de 'phral bka' shag sogs mi drag rnams dang /
gdan sa'i mkhan slob sogs ser skya spyi mgrin gcig gis /
rgyal dbang rin po che dgung lo nyi shu bzhes yod gshis /
chab srid kyi las 'gan bzhes dgos zhes zhus na'ang /
khong gis gsan bsam gyi 'phro skyong dgos gsungs nas zhal gyis ma bzhes /
de nas rgyud stod mkhan zur tsha rdor ngag dbang tshul khrims rgya nag tu chos spel bzhin bzhugs yod pa la gong mas no mon han gyi mtshan gnas gnang ba dang 'brel gdan 'dren zhus te srid skyong rgyal bor bskos /
khong gi 'khrungs yul ni a mdo co ne red /
dbus su slob gnyer byed du phyin nas se ra smad du grwa sar zhugs /
bzhugs gnas tsha rdor khang tshan yin 'dug slob gnyer bgyis te slar rgyud stod du phebs /
bla ma dbu mdzad dang /
de rjes mkhan po mdzad /
rjes su pe cin la slob dpon du gzhung gis mngags /
lcang skya rol ba'i rdo rje dang thugs snang mthun pa la brten /
gong ma chen lung gis kyang gzigs pa che /
me bya lo'i zla tshes nyin lha sar phebs skabs lha sa'i mi dmangs khri phrag mang bo ltad mor 'dus nas sngar gyi rgyud pa'i dge bshes grwa rkyang zhig glo bur du bod kyi srid skyong du phebs 'dug ces ha las nas blta bar yong ba red zer /
rjes su dga' ldan khri bar yang phebs /

gung kun dga' bstan 'dzin /
thon pa srid zhi dbang 'dus /

gong ma rang nyid dgung lo bdun cur phebs pa'i dga' ston dang 'brel chos rgya che ba zhu rgyu'i don du /

de nas rim gyis sku 'bum du phebs nas zla ba bzhi dang /

de skabs 'jam dbyangs bzhad sprul ma hA paN Di ta dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang bo'i phyag mdzod chen mo sogs zhabs gras lha 'brum gyis ma thar ba sum brgya skor la 'brum sman btab pas lam lhong chen po byung /
de nas zla tshes nyin zhe hor la phebs 'byor byung /
de nas pe cin du gong ma chen lung dang mjal 'phrad gnang /
tshes nyin zhe hor bkra shis lhun por phebs /
rab gnas mdzad /
zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes nyer lnga'i nyin zhe hor bkra shis lhun po nas pe cin du chibs bsgyur /
tshes nyer bdun nyin gong ma chen lung la mgon po'i rjes gnang sogs chos bka' ci rigs gnang /
lcags byi lo'i zla tshes nyin nyi rgas tsam la gzugs sku chos dbyings su thim /
lcags glang lo'i zla tshes nyin sku gdung gdan 'dren zhus te sku 'khor rnams pe cin nas chas te /
zla tshes nyin gdan sa bkra shis lhun por 'byor to / /

gung paN Di ta dang /
mda' dpon lcang lo can sogs kyis bod dmag gtos che ba drangs nas lcags byi lo'i zla nang sa ngan rdzong 'bur mo mer bsregs /
jag gtso sde rong a tshogs dang /
ru shod rta rgod byams pa pha bu sogs nyes can rnams sa gnas de gar srog chad khrag sbyor dang gzhan mang bo zhig rgyang 'phud btang /
lo der hal ha rje btsun dam pa'i sprul sku thugs brtag bcad /
lcags glang lo'i zla tshes nyin rgyal dbang mchog gis gsan bsam grub par brten chos srid lugs gnyis kyi thugs 'gan bzhes rung /
rgyun du chos phyogs kho nar nyams bzhes gnang stabs /
srid kyi las don la khri rin po che tsha rdor no mon han gyis las 'gan bzhes /
de'i phyi lor skyid grong bsam gtan gling nas mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang phyug dka' chen ye shes rgyal mtshan yongs 'dzin du gdan 'dren zhus nas rgyun du rtse pho brang chen mor bzhugs nas bka' chos rgyun ma chad par gnang /
pe cin nas rgyal dbang rin po cher gser gyi glegs bu bcu bdun thog yig rigs bzhi brkos kyi 'ja' sa 'bul mi 'byor /
shing 'brug lor nor gling bskal bzang pho brang gsar bzhengs mdzad /
tsha rdor no mon han zhes bod kyi rgyal bo grags pa can 'di ni lo ngo bcur bod kyi rgyal srid skyong bar bzhugs shing /
khong ni chos srid gnyis char mkhyen rgya che la rgya bod kyi dpon rigs gnon zil che zhing mi ser la shin tu byams pa sogs kyi dbang gis mtho dman kun gyis brtsi mthong che /
'di ba'i ring la tshong las sogs dpal 'byor dar rgyas che zhing /
dmangs kyi 'tsho ba'ang ha cang bzang ba dang /

de skabs pe cin du lcang skya rol ba'i rdo je sku gshegs stabs /
pe cin chos kyi slob grwa'i dbu 'dzin dang rgya nag gi nang ba sangs rgyas pa'i dgon pa yongs la bka' slob kyi ched du rgya nag pe cin du gdan drangs pa ltar /
me rta lo'i zla tshes la lha sa nas btegs te pe cin du phebs /
gong mas sa ma ti pak+Shi zhes pa'i go gnas gnang ste pe cin du bzhugs /
bod du rta tshag rje drung bstan pa'i mgon po la no mon han gyi cho lo dang bcas rgyal bor bskos 'dug go / /
me lug lo'i zla pa'i nang zhwa dmar ba sku phreng bcu ba chos 'grub rgya mtsho'i g.yog po karma mchog sbyin zer bas lam khrid byas te glo bur du bal bo gor Sha'i dmag gis btsan 'dzul byas te gnya' nang /
rong shar /
skyid grong ste rdzong gsum blangs /
rim gyis sa dga' sogs kyang blangs /
bod dmag gis mu mthud nas 'gog rgol byas /
rgya nag nas kyang dpon dmag 'bor chen 'byor yang 'gog rgol ma byas par chings brgyab /
chings don rdzong gsum tshur blu rin la rgya dngul rdo tshad sum brgya tham pa 'phral du sprad na rdzong gsum mkhregs bzung mi byed par bod la rtsis sprod byed byas te chings bar du rgya dpon rnams bsdad nas /
btsan shed kyis chings yig cig bod kyi mgo la bzhag blu rin kha shas sprad nas gor dmag rnams phyir log lo gsum gyi ring gor dmag gis 'phrog bcom byas pa'i mi dmangs la skyob gso byas /
skyid grong bsam gtan gling gor dmag gis bcom ste dge 'dun pa phal che ba lha sar phebs yod stabs /
yongs 'dzin ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi thugs dgongs ltar lcags khyi lor lha sa'i skyid chu'i lho phyogs tshe mchog gling gi dgon pa btab /
bod du stod phyogs gor dmag gis bcom pa dang /
dbus gtsang mdo khams sogs kyi rgya dmag gi 'gro lam gyi mi ser rnams thor ba dang /

skabs der srid 'dzin sde drug blo bzang mkhyen rab thugs gshis 'jam pas /
spyi khyab dpal ldan don 'grub dang /
dga' 'bras drung spyis dbang shed kyis gzhung sa'i zhabs 'bring dang 'bangs la brdab gsig chen po byung yod zer /

dbus su grwa sar yong nas dga' ldan shar rtse grwa tshang du tshogs zhugs byas /
khang tshan rdo khang dang /
mi tshan rmi li mi tshan khong red zer /
smon lam skabs shig bshad sgrar bka' 'gyur dang /

de rjes dga' ldan shar rtse mkhan po'i phyag mdzod du bskos /
bka' blon zur ba bshad sgra snye mo rgyal byed tshal du btson du bcug skabs srid skyong r+wa sgreng la ngo log gi las 'gul shugs chen brtsams te bshad sgra bskyar log gi las ka'i gtso bo kho red zer /
bar skabs shig la dga' ldan phyag mdzod sna bo che zhes grags pa che zhing dbang shugs che bar gyur /
sngar kho rang gi phyogs gtogs yin pa'i zhabs pad phu lung ba de yang /

kho'i gong du shor dogs pa red kyang zer /
gang ltar srar rdzong rdzong dpon la bka' shog phab nas chur bskyur te bsad /
dga' ldan phyag mdzod sna bo che dpal ldan don 'grub kyis dga' ldan dang 'bras spungs kyi mi chen dag kho'i rgyab la yod snyam nas bod ljongs yongs la dbang bsgyur rgyu'i ham sems skyes te /
rgyal dbang rin po che pha bong kha lta bu'i ri khrod cig la gsol phogs dang bcas 'jog rgyu byed rtsis dang /
srid skyong sde drug blo bzang mkhyen rab kyi srid skyong gi go gnas bshol thabs kyi bya ba byas /
zhabs pad gsar byung bskal bzang dgra 'dul dang mtsho sgo ba mig dmar tshe ring /
bshad sgra tshe ring dbang phyug b+h+rum pa rnam rgyal rdo rje bcas kyang dpal don gyis zil gyis mnan yod /

srid skyong phyag mdzod kyis dpal don la bshad de bya shor nas /
dpal don gyis mtsho sgo ba la dogs pa zos pa dang /
b+h+rum pa la yang dogs pa zos nas de gnyis med par byed snyam pa skyes /

dgongs zhu gnang dgos zhes /
nga tshos skul ma btang na ji 'dra zhes bsam 'char dris par /

rjes sor lkog gsod byas pa ha go nas /

rang yul du 'bros grabs byas kyang /
dga' ldan gyi mi chen dag gis /
dga' ldan du drangs nas srung skyob byas mod /
sde gzhung bka' shag gis lha sar yod pa'i dmag dngos gzhi btang ste dga' ldan gyi mtha' skor nyin shas la dmag 'thab byas mthar /

dpal don gyi ro dang /

'di skor la /
mkhas pa 'ga' zhig dang dpon rigs 'ga' zhig gis dbyin lugs kyi gsar brje byed dgos tshul gong ma kwang zhu la zhus par kwang zhus khas blangs par tshi shis tha'i hus ngo rgol byas te gong ma bzang btson du bcug bzi sprid kyi dug drangs te tshor dbang nyams par byas /
gsar brje'i gros 'don mkhan gyi mkhas pa 'ga' zhig phyi rgyal du bros /
mkhas pa 'ga' zhig dang dpon rigs 'ga' zhig bzung nas bsad pa sogs kyis gsar brje'i bya bar pham nyes byung ba sogs bris 'dug rgyal dbang mchog rgya sog gi yul du lo ngo bzhi lhag la bzhugs skabs phyi rgyal gyi dpon rigs mang bor thug 'phrad bka' mol gyis srid don mi nyung ba re thag bcad pa dang /

de'i nub mor rgyal dbang 'khor bcas bros byol mi byed mthu med byung /
rgya dmag gis ra mda' rjes 'ded byas kyang ma zin par rgya gar du slebs /
lo 'di'i dgun thog rgyal dbang rin po che 'khor bcas rgya bal gyi gnas rten khag la gnas gzigs su phebs /
rgya gar shar phyogs kyi nang ba'i mchod rten khag dang /
sangs rgyas sku 'khrungs pa'i gnas bal yul gyi mnga' khongs su lum+bi ni dang /
sangs rgyas pa'i gnas rdo rje gdan sogs su gnas mjal du phebs /
lcags phag lo'i zla ba nas rgya'i dpon dmag nang tshags 'khrug zing gsod res yang yang byed pa dang /
rgya nag pe cin du sun krong hran gyi gsar brje byung ste shon thong khri las phab pa'i gsar 'gyur thon byung stabs ko lo'i hu'i khongs gtogs kyi rgya dmag rnams kyis man ching dpon rigs tshor ngo log brgyab /
kra'o ar phung gi las khungs lte ba chab mdor brgyab yod kyang 'dug ma bzod par khrin tur phyin /
de'i phyi lo kho rang khrin tu nas bsad /
bod kyi sa gnas so so nas rgya dmag la rgyab rten med par shes nas ngo rgol dang dpung 'jug byas /
rgya dmag rnams kyang rgya yul du 'gro 'dod skyes te bod gzhung la lam dngul sogs dgos zer ba ltar bod gzhung gis lam gyi mi ser la brdab gsig mi 'byung ched dngul srang chig 'bum brgyad khri byin /
dngul la lag tu 'byor mtshams nga rgyal skyes te 'gro rgyu phar zad bcom 'phrog byed rgyu'i gros ngan byas te /
chu byi lo'i zla tshes la se rar dpung 'jug byas nas nyin gsum la gtugs kyang se rar 'dzul ma thub /
se ra'i mtha' skor gyi ri khrod dang dgon chung rnams la me btang nas bsregs /
dmag rnams se ra nas 'then te lha sar 'dzul /
rgya bod kyi dmag gi g.yul 'gyed drag po zla ngo kha shas la brgyab /
sa ga zla ba'i nang du grwa ba kha shas dang /
bod dmag kha shas rtse pho brang nang du bka' shag gi tshogs 'du 'tshogs yod pa'i thog tu brgyugs nas bka' blon rnams bzung /
rtse zhol du khrid nas /
tsha rong ba dbang phyug rgyal bo dang /
tsha rong sras /
bka' drung tsha gur zhag pa /
mkhan drung phun rab pa /
bla phyag mkhan chung bsam mkhar ba /
rtse drung blo bzang rdo rje rnams la me mda' brgyab nas bsad /
bka' tshab bla ma bstan 'dzin chos grags /
bka' tshab ram pa ba /
glang gdong ba bcas kyang re zhig zhol las khungs su bzang brtson byas nas bzhag pa red zer /
'di dag gis rgya mi dang 'brel ba byas pa red zer nas bsad pa dang /
btson 'jug byas pa red zer 'dug zhib cha sus shes /
dus de tsam na yon hri khe'i srid gzhung gis lha sar sdod pa'i man ching am ban lin yu 'phral du phyir log dgos pa dang /
dmag dpon cung yun gyis am ban gyi las 'gan sngar ltar 'khur dgos pa sogs kyi bka' phab /
rgya dmag rnams la dmag snon dang dmag rgyags sogs med par dka' tshegs ha cang che stabs phyir log 'dod che ba byung /
rgya'i zhi drag dpon rigs rnams kyis bod dmag la mgo sgur /
mgo btags chings yig bzhag mthar chu byi lo'i zla tshes la rgya dmag yongs rdzogs 'gro dgos byung ba red /
bstan rgyas gling bla brang gis rgya dmag dang lag 'brel byas par brten /
bla brang dang ban grwa tshang bcas gtan med byas pa red /
lo 'khor gcig la dmag 'khrug brgyab stabs lha sa grong khyer sum cha gcig tsam gtor bshigs byas pa sogs skyon chen po byung /
chu byi lo'i zla tshes nyin rgyal dbang rin po che rtse pho brang chen por phebs 'byor byung /
de ltar lo ngo gsum yas mas shig la rgya gar sogs su phebs mthar slar gdan sar zhabs sor 'khod rgyu byung ngo / /
lha sar phebs nas 'phral du rtsa tshig cig bsgrigs nas /
chu glang lo'i zla tshes nyin sbyar 'grem gnang ba dang 'brel /
gzhung zhabs go gnas sogs bskyar 'dems dang tshar gcod rjes 'dzin skabs su gang bab gnang zhing shog lor gsar ba bzo 'grem byas /
chu glang lo nas yig skyel sbrag zam gsar ba btsugs /
gzhung zhabs kyi phru gu bzhi ing lan rags ba'i zhes pa'i slob grwar slob sbyong du btang /
de ni dga' ldan pho brang ba'i skabs bod mi phyi rgyal du slob sbyong la 'gro mi dang bo red /
sgog mkhar ba bsod nams mgon po dmag las slob sbyong la 'jar man du mngags /
chu glog gsar 'dzugs gnang ste /
grwa bzhi thang du me mda'i bzo grwa /
dngul par khang /
shog dngul par 'debs khang sogs btsugs /
lha sa'i dar 'phrin las khungs yang yar rgyas btang /
shing stag lo rgya bod dbyin gsum gyis chings yig bzhag shing yos lor dmag dpon dang dmag gi 'god sgrig gnang /
lo 'di'i yas mas su paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa chos kyi nyi ma mchog nas bkra shis lhun por gser zangs las grub pa'i rgyal ba byams pa'i sku brnyan 'dzam gling du sngar byung ma myong ba'i chen po gcig bzhengs /
me 'brug lor dmag sbyong dang dmag dpung lam lugs gsar ba gsar 'dzugs byas /
de mtshungs mi drug tsam zhig rgya gar du dmag 'thab lag rtsal sbyong du mngags /
bstan rgyas gling gi nye 'gram du sman rtsis rig gnas khang gsar skrun gnang /
se ra sman sbyin mkhyen rab nor bur sman rtsis mkhan chung du bsko gzhag gnang ngo / /
de lo nas mdo khams stod du bod dmag dang rgya dmag gi g.yul 'gyed thengs du mar byas /
mthar gyod bshad de chings yig bzhag bal yul mchod rten rnam gsum zhig gso mdzad /
lcags sprel lor bu ston gsung 'bum dang /
rgyal ba'i bka' 'gyur ro cog gi par bskrun rgyu'i 'go bzung /
bka' 'gyur rin po che'i par shing bzhugs yul rtse pho brang chen po'i zhol du gtsug lag rten gtso byams sku chen po bcas lo 'khor bzhi'i ring la legs par grub /
gzhung sa'i dpon rigs dag gis byed las sna tshogs la brten /
paN chen thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang chos kyi nyi ma ston 'khor bcas /
chu phag lo'i zla tshes la bkra shis lhun po nas chas te sog yul brgyud rgya nag tu phebs pa dang /
sog yul dang mdo khams rnams su 'gro don rgya chen po gnang /
chu phag lor rgyal rtser dbyin yig gi slob grwa gsar 'dzugs gnang ste lo gsum tsam song rjes /
gdan sa gsum gyi slob dpon las snes dbyin yig gi slob grwa btsugs na mi 'grig tshul shugs chen pos zhus pa ltar slob grwa phyir 'then mi byed mthu med byung /
shing bya lor lha ldan drung spyi'i gling khar slob grwa gsar 'dzugs kyis /
dbyin yig dang bod yig slob pa'i slob grwa btsugs mod /
'dzam gling gi gnas tshul mi shes pa dag gis chos lugs la gnod ces ngo rgol byas rkyen slob grwa phyir bsdu gnang ste /
bu phrug skya ser 'ga' zhig bod gzhung gis 'gro song btang nas rdo rje gling gi san jo seb ces pa'i slob grwar gtong gnang mdzad /
skabs de dus shig nas deng rabs kyi dmag sbyong dang dmag sgrig sogs la ched gnyer mdzad /
shing byi lor lha zhol grong khyer nang khrims srung dmag mi gsar 'dzugs gnang ste /
'phrod bsten gtsang spra dang /
rkun jag bde 'jags sogs la lta rtog byas pas phan pa chen po byung /
me stag lor phag ri nas rgyal rtse bar rlangs 'khor 'gro lam bzos te rlangs 'khor bzhi tsam slebs pas /
mi ser sogs nas phyugs zog rta drel sogs 'drogs nas brdabs chag dang bor stor byung 'dug rlangs 'khor phyir 'then byed rogs zhes nan zhus byas pa ltar rlangs 'khor phyir 'then mi byed mthu med byung /
sa 'brug lo nas lha sa dang grwa bzhi glog 'phrul khang sogs su phebs skabs rlangs 'khor che chung bzhi tsam bde spyad de rim gyis bod mi'i mig lam du 'dris cha byung mtshams rgya khyab tu spel rgyu'i thugs dgongs gnang /
lcags lug lo nas grwa bzhi glog 'phrul khang gsar 'dzugs gnang ste /
zangs dang dngul gyi Tam kha dang shog dngul tshon khra ma sogs par 'debs dang /
me mda' /
rdzas med la sogs bzo skrun gyi grwa rgya che btsugs shing /
sa sprul lo yas mas su sa 'du tshang dang be ri dpon ma mthun par dmag 'khrug langs nas be ri dpon gyis rgya dmag khrid 'ongs nas rgya bod dmag gi 'khrug zing langs te /
bod dmag re zhig rgyal /
lcags lug lor slar yang zi khron rgya dmag slebs te bod dmag gis ma thub par hor brag mgo rgya lag tu shor /
rgya dmag gis dar rgyas dgon pa rtsa gtor btang /
hor khog dang /
nyag rong gnyis ka sa shor te bod dmag la pham nyes che ba byung stabs chu sprel lo'i zla pa'i nang chings mi rgyag mthu med byung /
skabs de dang dus mtshungs su zi ling nas mA pi h+phang gi dmag nang chen sa khul du 'byor te bod dmag dang 'thab rtsod byas pas thog mar bod dmag rgyal ba 'dra yang phyis su bod dmag pham nas phyir 'then byed dgos byung /
chu sprel lo de'i zla pa'i nang ldan khog tu zi khron rgya dmag slebs nas /
bod dmag la pham nyes byung ste phyir 'then byas /
lo 'dir lho byang gnyis ka nas bod dmag la pham nyes byung /
chu bya lo'i zla tshes nyin spre tsha dgon du zi ling gi mA pi h+phang gi srid tshab dang chings yig bzhag chu sprel lor gnas chung chos skyong chen po'i lung bstan bzhin brtan bzhugs phul ba'i gsung lan rnam thar du 'dug chu bya lo'i zla bo'i nang yang srid bka' lhan rgyas kyis zhu ba phul ba'i gsung lan la bltas na /
de'i dus chab srid 'gan 'khur ba dag gis thugs bzhed dang mthun pa zhig byed kyin med 'dug lo de'i zla ba bcu ba'i tshes shar nas sku snyun bzhes pa rim gyis je lcir song ste /
zla ba bcu ba'i tshes sum cu'i nyin gzugs sku chos dbyings su thim mo / /
de ma thag snyog gra langs te /
sku bcar kun 'phel lags kyis rgyal dbang sku bsnyun pa gsang rgya byas nas /
gzhung zhabs la ma bshad zer ba sogs kyi nag nyes btsal nas /
sku bcar kun 'phel dang /
bkra shis don 'grub /
em chi byams pa /
gnas chung sku rten sogs gnas dbyung byas pa sogs chab srid nyams rgud kyi rtags mtshan mngon du gyur 'dug go / /
rgyal dbang bcu gsum pa chen po gshegs nas zla ba gnyis tsam la srid bka' lhan rgyas nas gzhung don bsgrubs /
de nas srid 'dzin rgyal tshab cig dgos tshul gros bsdur byas te /
dga' ldan khri ba las thog pa mi nyag a mi ye shes dbang ldan dang /
r+wa sgreng ho thog thu 'jam dpal ye shes bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan /
phur lcog yongs 'dzin sprul sku thub bstan byams pa tshul khrims gsum gyi mtshan shog zan ril bsgril nas rtse 'phags mchog lo ke shwa ra'i spyan sngar srid bka' /
drung rtsis /
tshogs 'thus bcas pa'i dbus su dga' ldan khri zur byams pa chos grags sang gis thugs smon bden tshig brjod bzhin zan rtags bsgril bas r+wa sgreng ho thog thu thon pa ltar shing khyi lo'i zla tshes nyin rgyal tshab kyi khrir phebs /
de nas ring bo ma song bar /
rtsis dpon lung shar gyis 'go khrid pa'i gzhung zhabs mang bo zhig zur 'tshogs byed pa'i gnas tshul thon /
lung shar de ni phyi rgyal du 'dug myong bas yar thon rgyal khab kyi lam lugs mthong stabs /
gsar brje'i bcos bsgyur byed rgyu byas pa red zer srol 'dug gang ltar rtsis dpon lung shar sogs 'dzin bzung dang /
lung shar gyi mig bton /
gzhan dag gnas dbyung sogs kyi khrims bcad /
rgyal dbang bcu gsum pa'i gser gdung rin po che thog tshad lnga yod pa lo 'khor gnyis la legs par grub /
rgyal dbang bcu gsum pas spom mda' stobs rgyal la rmar khams khul gyi yul dmag gi ru dpon du bsko gzhag gnang ste sa mtshams su yod par /
rgyal dbang gshegs rjes sku bcar kun 'phel do dam thog rgyang 'phud btang tshul thos 'phral ma dga' bar shing khyi lo'i zla nang kho rang gi 'og la yod pa'i yul dmag rnams khrid de rmar khams sa srung cha dang mda' dpon nor rgyas nang ba'i dmag sgar thog mtshan 'gebs ngo log byas te brgya dpon dang /
dmag mi kha shas rmas skyon dang /
spyi sger gyi rgyu dngos dang mtshon cha sogs phrogs /
ru dpon stobs rgyal dang /
spun rgan pa rab dga' gnyis kyis khams phyogs tshang ma bod gzhung 'og nas 'bud dgos pa'i yi ge bkram mod don 'bras smin khom ma byung 'dug la /
chab mdo nas bod dmag thon skabs 'ba' phyogs su bros /
de skabs 'ba' phyogs de rgya lag tu yod stabs bod dmag der 'gro thabs bral /
rgyal dbang bcu bzhi ba rtsad gcod ched /
shing phag lo'i zla nang rgyal tshab r+wa sgreng ho thog thu sogs lha mo'i bla mtshor gzigs zhib la phebs /
mtsho nang nas dbu can gyi yi ge a dang /
ka ma zhes dang /
dgon pa thog sa sum rtseg bar thog g.yu rtsi can gyi yang steng gser zangs kyi rgya phibs yod pa /
dgon pa de'i shar phyogs 'gro lam skya thal le ri chung zhig gi rtsar thug pa /
de'i thad khang ba thog gcig ma thog sngon po byas pa gcig shar 'dug gsungs /
shing phag lor bod gzhung gi gtso bo dag gis gros bsdur gyis paN chen rin po che rgya yul du bzhugs pa gdan 'dren zhus pa yin mod /
go min tang srid gzhung gis paN chen rin po che bod yul du phebs tshe phebs skyel du rgya dpon che ba kha shas dang /
sku srung dmag mi lnga brgya bcas gtong rgyu yin tshul dang /
paN chen rin po cher nub phyogs kyi yon tan khyad par can gyi mnga' bdag ces pa'i mtshan gsol ba sogs bod gzhung gis khas ma blangs pa sogs 'gal rkyen sna tshogs kyi dbang gis paN chen rin po che bod du phebs rgyur 'gyangs 'gor byung zhing /
me glang lo'i zla tshes la paN chen rin po che skye dgu mdo'i don 'grub gling zhes pa'i dgon par sku mya ngan las 'das so / /
de skabs nyi hong ri pin gis rgya yul du btsan 'dzul byed sgang yin pas paN chen sku gdung rin po che hor khog tu gdan drangs nas dkar mdzes dgon du bzhugs /
sa stag lor li'u wun hus dang /
paN chen zhabs 'bring ba rnams ma mthun par zing 'khrug langs te sku chas rnams rgya dmag gi lag tu shor yang /
sku gdung rin po che gdan sa bkra shis lhun por gdan 'dren thub pa byung /
sa stag lo'i zla tshes nyin srid 'dzin r+wa sgreng ba'i thugs dgongs ltar srid blon glang mdun zur bzhugs byas te /
r+wa sgreng gis srid dbang yongs rdzogs bzung /
rgyal dbang sku phreng bcu bzhi ba bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho /
rgyal dbang bcu bzhi ba ni /
sku 'bum byams pa gling gi nye 'dabs stag 'tsher zhes pa'i sde ba'i nang du yab chos skyong tshe ring dang yum bsod nams mtsho gnyis la rab byung bcu drug pa'i shing phag lo'i zla tshes la sku 'khrungs /
mtshan lha mo don 'grub zer /
'di ba lha mo mtsho gzigs kyi lung bstan dang /
chos skyong dang /
paN chen rin po ches kyang thugs dgongs yod pa dang /
ke tshang sprul sku sogs kyis brtag dpyad sogs gang cha nas ngos 'dzin 'khrul med byung zer /
de nas bod ljongs su gdan 'dren zhu skabs 'khrungs yul mA pi h+phang gi 'og tu yod gshis /
mA pi h+phang la blu yon dngul sgor 'bum bzhi snga rjes su sprad nas gdan drangs te /
sa yos lo'i zla tshes nyin nor gling bskal bzang pho brang du zhabs sor 'khod /
zla tshes nyin gtsug lag khang du r+wa sgreng ho thog thus gtsug phud bzhes te mtshan rje btsun 'jam dpal ngag dbang blo bzang ye shes bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho srid gsum dbang bsgyur mtshungs pa med pa'i sde dpal bzang bo zhes mtshan gsol /
lcags 'brug lo'i zla tshes nyin pho brang po ta la'i khrir phebs /
khrir phebs kyi mdzad sgo lugs srol bzhin mdzad /
lcags 'brug lo'i zla nang rgyal tshab r+wa sgreng gis las 'khur dgongs zhu gnang /
lcags sbrul lo'i zla tshes nyin yongs 'dzin stag brag ngag dbang gsung rab mthu stobs bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan srid skyong gi khrir phebs /
chu rta lo'i zla tshes nyin lha ldan gtsug lhag khang gi mdun du rgyal dbang gis srid skyong stag brag gi drung nas rab byung gi sdom pa bzhes /

a ri dang /
dbyin ji dang /
go min tang srid gzhung rnams la rgyal kha thob par dga' ston zhu mi dza sag thub bstan bsam 'phel sogs mngags /
spyi sger gyi bun skyed shin tu lci bas mi ser rnams ni bya rgan sgro zad du gyur te 'tsho thabs bral ba'i skabs su shing sprel lor bod gzhung tshogs 'du nas mi ser la brdab gsig de 'dra byed mi chog pa sogs kyi bka' rgya bkram /
shing bya lo'i ston dus 'phan po lhun 'grub rdzong du ser byas grwa tshang dang /
sngags pa grwa tshang gi 'bru len rnams kyis snga dus bzhin gyi skyed kha chen po len pa mi ser rnams kyis bod gzhung gi bka' gsar ltar las ma sprad par lhun 'grub rdzong dpon la gtug bsher byas pas rdzong dpon gyis bka' gsar ltar byed dgos zhes mi ser gyi rgyab rtsa byas stabs 'bru gnyer rnams kyis rdzong dpon nyes rdung btang ste bsad /
byed gte rnams la nyes chad bcad par /
ser byas sngags gnyis kyis de dag gi rgyab rtsa byas pa sogs kyis zing cha byung zer /
lo de'i zla dgu bar lha klu tshe dbang rdo rje la rdzong rgyab tu lkog mda' 'phangs te rta bsad zer /

bka' blon zur khang dang /
lha klu gnyis kyi dmag brgya skor zhig khrid nas r+wa sgreng dgon nas rgyal zur r+wa sgreng ho thog thu 'khor bcas bzung ste rtser khrid song zer /
r+wa sgreng gis go min tang la'ang lag 'brel byas te srid skyong stag brag khri las 'phen thabs byas song yang zer /
gang ltar de nyin r+wa sgreng bla brang dang /
yab gzhis phun tshogs khang gsar dang /
sa 'du tshang rnams la sgo rgya byas song zer /
ser byas sngags gnyis kyi mkhan po snga ma gnyis tsha len byas te gsar bzhag byas yod stabs /
tshes nyin ser byas mkhan po gsar pa blo bzang bstan dar ngo g.yog bzhi ser byas grwa ba kha shas kyis bsad zer /
tshes nyin rgyal zur r+wa sgreng dang /
mkhar rdo sprul sku /
smyung gnas bla ma blo bzang ye shes rnam rgyal /
r+wa sgreng sku tsha dza sag sogs la 'dri gcod byas par rgyal zur tshang nas /
smyung mkhar dza gsum gyis snga rjes su srid skyong la lkog ngan byed rgyu'i skul ma btang ba /
rgyal zur tshang gis de ltar byed mi nyan gsungs par ma zad kha ta go bskon byas pa'i yi ge phar tshur bskur ba rnams smyung gnas bla ma'i sgo chung nang nas thon te /
rgyal zur tshang nas khas len dngos gtsang gnang ba dang /
khong la nyes nag med 'dug zer gyin 'dug zer /

lag 'bom yod pa'i sgam de 'bul mkhan kho yin /

sil ma bzhi bcu la sogs par gyur pa'i skabs shig bod spyi'i rgyal bo'i thog ma gnya' khri btsan pos gangs can gyi bod rus chen bzhi sogs gcig gyur byas te dbang bsgyur ba sogs gong du brjod zin la /
de yang dbus gtsang la bod dang /
stod mnga' ris nas smad mdo khams kyi bar la bod chen po zer /
smad mdo khams la mdo stod dang mdo smad gnyis byas pa'i mdo smad la a mdo zer ba'i rgyu mtshan ni /
mdo smad chos 'byung las /
"'bri chu'i se bo'i lung ring brgal ba'i ba yan ha ri'i shar ngos a chen gangs rgyab kyi ri dang /
mdo la gnyis kyi ming bsdoms pas de man chad la a mdo zer /
de ngos kyi chu rnams phyogs 'dres kyi rma g.yang phyug mo'i gzhung du 'bab pa la rma chur grags pa mtsho so lo ma'am skya rengs kyi gzhung brgyud lho phyogs su 'khyog pa'i khug so man chad a mdo nyid la ngos 'dzin dgos pa ni /
chol kha gsum du phye tshe /
mnga' ris gung thang nas sog la skya bo yan chad dbus gtsang chos kyi chol kha /
de nas rma chu'i khug pa yan mdo stod mi'i chol kha /
de nas rgya'i mchod rten dkar bo yan mdo smad rta'i chol khar byed pas shes so / /
" zhes gsungs pa ltar ro / /
'di la'ang phyis kyi rtog bzo mkhan 'ga' zhig gis rtog bzo byas pa yod mod kyang /
don la 'di ltar yin no / /
mdo smad 'dir yang bod rgyal dag gi mnga' 'bangs bod mis khyab nas rim gyis dar zhing rgyas pa'i skabs su /
shar phyogs kyi rgyal bo dag gis nub phyogs su rgya bskyed pa dang /
khyad par thang gi rgyal bo u te sogs kyi skabs mdo smad kyi sa sne dag tu dmag 'bor chen btang ste /
bod mi dag gsod 'ded byas nas /
kru'u zer ba'i dmag gi gzhi sa brgya lhag btsugs /
mkhar du ma brtsigs te re zhig gzhis chags /
bod kyi gtam dpe la rgya zhag gcig 'dug sar mkhar brtsigs zhes zer /
de rjes srong btsan gyi skabs bod dmag 'bum phrag du ma mngags te /
thang dmag rang yul du bskrad nas so mtshams srung ba'i dmag ches mang bo bzhag mdo khams nags dang na'i ljongs de bod rang gi lag tu thob ste /
bod kyi btsan po dag gis dbang bsgyur /
de rjes glang dar ma'i byed spyod ngan pa'i stabs kyis /
'bangs gyen log byung ste bod sil bur thor mod /
stod mnga' ris su glang dar gyi sras rtsod med gnam lde 'od srung gi rgyal rgyud rnams kyis rgyal bo byas te rgya bal gyi sa mtshams srung zhing /
chos dang rig gnas sogs dar bar byas pa'i phyag rjes shin tu rlabs che ba yin no / /
dang bo /
mdo smad kyi lo rgyus las tsong kha'i rgyal bo'i skor /
mdo smad tsong kha'i yul du /
bod kyi rgyal rgyud tsong kha'i rgyal bo zer ba'i rgyal bo stobs ldan zhig byung nas /
da lta'i zi ling mkhar du rgyal sa bzung ste mtha' mtshams brtan por srung /
'di ba bod kyi rgyal rgyud yin pa /
sung gi lo rgyus sogs rgya'i yig deb rnams gcig mthun yin zhing /
mtshan la'ang jo sras sam rgyal sras zhes zer /
'di'i rgyud pa ni bod kyi rgyal rgyud cig yin zer ba las /
byung tshul la rgya'i deb ther la lar shin cang nas bod kyi rgyal bo'i rgyud pa'i sras shig spyan drangs pa yin zer ba dang /
yang 'ga' zhig gis yar lung jo bo'i rgyud pa zhig yin zer ba'ang snang mod /
phyi ma 'di ni rgyal rabs gsal ba'i me long las /
yum brtan gyi rgyud pa yar lung du chags pa yar lung jo bor grags pa rnams kyi rgyud rabs bshad pa'i skabs su /
" nyi ma mgon gyi sras nyi 'od dpal mgon /
'di'i brgyud rlung shod /
'phan yul /
mdo khams na mang ngo " zhes gsungs pa tsam la brten par snang /
snga ma ni shin cang zer mod /
stod mnga' ris dang shin cang khad nye zhing /
shin cang yang bar skabs shig tu bod kyi chab 'og tu gtogs pas /
mnga' ris dang shin cang khyad ma phye bar 'dra ste /
rgyal sras 'di ni stod mnga' ris phyogs nas 'ongs pa yin te /
glang dar gyi sras rtsod med gnam lde 'od srung gi sras mnga' bdag dpal 'khor btsan /
de la sras khri bkra shis brtsegs pa dang /
skyid lde nyi ma mgon gnyis /
khri bkra shis brtsegs pa la sras dpal lde /
'od lde /
skyid lde gsum /
'bring bo 'od lde la sras pha ba lde /
khri lde /
khri chung /
nyag pa bzhi yod pa'i gnyis pa khri lde ni mdo khams su byon pa de yin par gsal /
deb ther dpyid kyi rgyal mo'i glu dbyangs las " gnyis pa mdo smad tsong khar yod cing " zhes dang /
deb ther dmar bo gsar ma las " sras gnyis pa khri lde'i rgyud ni /
shar tsong kha sogs mdo smad du chad de /
da lta'i lha don po che sa yang khri lde'i rgyud du me long mar bshad " ces dang /
deb ther dmar bo las " khri lde'i brgyud shar tsong kha'i rgyal bo spyan snga don chen la sogs pa mdo smad kyi rgyal rgyud rnams yin no " zhes dang /
rgya bod yig tshang las " shar tsong kha'i rgyal bo /
spyan snga don chen pa la sogs pa mdo smad kyi rgyal rgyud rnams yin no " zhes dang /
thu'u bkwan rnam thar las " bra'i sde che ba zhig dbus nas mdo smad du chad pa la bra sde zhes 'bod pa phyis su zur nyams nas bra sti zhes grags pa yin no / /
dbus nas chad tshul ni /
khri srong gi sras chung ba sad na legs mjing yon /
de'i sras dar ma /
de'i sras gnam lde 'od srung /
de'i sras mnga' bdag dpal 'khor btsan /
de'i sras khri bkra shis brtsegs pa dpal /
de'i sras 'od lde la sras bzhi byung ba'i gnyis pa khri lde 'bangs ha cang mi mang tsam dang bcas mdo smad du byon /
de dus bra sde'ang rgyal bo dang lhan du mdo smad du thon cing /
mtsho khri shog rgyal mo'i 'gram bod kyis bzung ste /
chos rgyal gdung rgyud des khri dpon mdzad cing /
bra nyang btsan bya bas rgyal bo'i blon gyi gtso bo byas tshul /
rus mdzod za 'og ma las byung /
rus mdzod der chos rgyal gyi gdung rgyud phyi ma ji ltar byung tshul mi gsal zhing /
bra sde'i rgyud pa byung tshul ni jo bo rje bod du ma byon pa'i gong tsam du bra sgom chos kyi rdo rje sku 'khrungs /
'di mtsho snying ma hA de war byon nas sgrub pa mdzad pas mngon shes dang rdzu 'phrul thob " ces dang /
" de dus mtsho 'gram gyi bod sde'i dpon ke khod rgya bya ba yin la /
'di chos rgyal gyi rgyud pa yin min gsal kha mi 'dug " ces dang /
" des khri dpon ke khod rgya dga' nas /
bra sgom la rta stong /
ri tshil dkar gyis gtsos pa'i 'bul chen phul te bla mar bkur /
bod 'bangs thams cad kyis bra sgom kho na bla mar bkur dgos pa'i dril bsgrags " zhes dang /
" skabs shig bra sde'i tshe phyug 'phan bya ba zhig bod kyi khri dpon la dbang bsgyur /
mi rabs kha shas kyi mtshams nas khri dpon gyi mnga' thang nyams pas /
tshe phyug 'phan gyi rgyud pa gle gshin bon dmar bya ba bon lugs kyi grub thob cig byung ba des bra sdes gtsos pa'i bod 'bangs mi nyung tsam khrid nas mdo smad kyi mtha' ri brag nags tshal yod pa'i gnas bzung " zhes gsungs /
mdo smad chos 'byung deb ther rgya mtsho las /
" khri bkra shis brtsegs pa'i sras 'od lde la sras bzhi byung ba'i gnyis pa khri lde mdo khams su phebs nas /
mtsho sngon 'dir gzhi bzung ste khri dpon mdzad /
tsong kha yul chen bco brgyad sogs mdo smad phal cher la mnga' mdzad pa'i rgyud du spyan snga don chen pa sogs byung bar bshad la /
da dung yang khri dpon de'i rgyud pa dpal ris phyogs su yod pa la /
'phan yul rang skad ma nyams pas khri dpon du 'bod pa yod snang /
" zhes gsungs so / /
des na khri lde tsong kha'i rgyal bor gyur nas so mtshams brtan srung byas pa'i lag rjes che /
win then krin zer bas bris pa'i rgya yig gi lo rgyus nang du " spyi lo nas lo'i bar rgya bod gnyis lan gru phyogs su 'khrugs nas bod mi khri drug tsam bsad /
rgya'i dmag dpon rang nyid kyang dmag thog tu bkrongs" zhes pa'ang tsong kha'i rgyal bo dang 'thab pa yin nges te /
spyi lo dang sbrags pa de yang dag pa yin na rab byung dang bo'i sa pho byi ba'i lo nas /
rab byung gnyis pa'i sa mo sbrul gyi bar khel yod /
de dus dbus gtsang sil bur thor te /
lung ba re la sde dpon re /
sde dpon re la btsan rdzong re /
rang sde srung ba'i dmag nyung shas re bsgrigs nas yod pa'i skabs red /
tsong kha'i rgyal bo 'dis kan su'u dang hra'an zhi'i sa cha 'ga' zhig bcas la dbang bsgyur /
shar phyogs kyi rgya dang byang phyogs kyi mi nyag la'ang g.yul 'gyed du ma byas /
mi nyag ni sbyir bod yin te /
mi nyag dang /
'brug pa rgyal bo gnyis /
bod rgyal gyi spun gnyis so sor khams kyi rgyal bo byas pa yin par /
'brug pa'i lo rgyus 'ga' dang /
rgya bod yig tshang nang du'ang bshad yod /
mi nyag ces pa mi nag ces sgra 'gyur ba yin par bshad /
tsong kha'i rgyal bo dang mi nyag rgyal bos sa khongs 'phrog res dang /
so so'i dar rgud kyi dbang gis sa mtshams mtha' gcig tu ngos zin dka' yang mdo smad chos 'byung las /
" phyi ma 'dis bal bo'i bla ma pham mthing ba mi nyag rgyal bo la dbang bskur ba'i bla ma gnang /
de'i dus mi nyag gi yul ni /
byang gi bod sog gi mtshams chu nag dang nye ba'i sar mi nyag rgyal bo'i thog ma si hu'i ga'i ju zhes pa byung ste rgya hor phal cher gyi bdag po byas /
shar na rgya nag lho na 'jang ? nub na bod /
byang hor gyis bcad pa'i dbus ni mi nyag gi rgyal khams te " zhes dang /
yang de las " g+ha dang byang ngos sogs ni yul gyi dngos gzhi yin la /
rab stod tshar sgang gi sa rnams kyang mi nyag la gtogs zhes bshad /
mi nyag rgyal rabs lnga ba the hus karma dus gsum mkhyen pa gdan 'dren zhus pa ma phebs par dge bshes gtsang bo sku tshab tu btang /
de'i sras mi nyag rgyal rgod yin par grags " zhes gsungs /
mi nyag g+ha zhes 'bod pa'i g+ha ni yul gyi ming yin par bshad /
mi nyag 'di rgyas tung khud dang /
tung shang zer la phyis su shas zha zer /
bod kyis mi nyag zer ba'i brda la brten nas /
deng sang gi rgya'i lo rgyus 'ga' zhig tu /
tung shang gi sbyang ? la bod kyis mi 'og zer mi nyag zer ba ma go ba red /
mi'i 'og ma tha chad du brtsi zhes bris pa khungs med kyi 'chal gtam mo / /
sung rgyal rabs byang mas ? mi nyag 'gog ched /
tsong kha'i rgyal bo la rgyu nor 'bor chen dang /
bya dga' ming btags sogs thengs du mar byin te 'brel ba bzang bo btsugs par /
sung gi lo rgyus las bshad /

khom long byung tshe zhib 'jug bya rtsis yin /
sung gis tsong kha'i rgyal bo la rgyal sras zer zhing /
'bangs mi rnams la bod ? zer la /
sung gi 'bangs mi rgya rigs yongs kyis sbyang ? zer /
tsong kha'i rgyal bos lo brgya yar mar la dbang bsgyur bar bshad /
skabs 'gar mi nyag ma gtogs pa'i mdo khams yongs la dbang bsgyur ba dang /
skabs 'gar tsong kha yul chen bco brgyad tsam la dbang bsgyur /
kho'i mnga' 'bangs kyi mi ni gtso bo bod mi yin la /
rgya dang sog po'ang mi nyung bar bshad /

gnyis pa /
mdo smad kyi lo rgyus las gling ge sar gyis dbang bsgyur tshul /
de dang dus rags pa mtshungs par /
mdo khams stod smad kyi sa mtshams su /
gling seng chen ge sar nor bu dgra 'dul zhes pa'i dpa' bo stobs ldan zhig gis /
phyogs bzhi'i dgra btul ba'i lo rgyus skad grags can yod la /
de'i 'byung khungs sogs ni bod kyi rus mdzad rnying ba dag tu gsal ba ltar bshad par bya ste /
bod kyi rus chen bzhi'i nang gi ldong la a spo ldong zhes zer la /
gna' sgrung las ldong che gnyan can zhes dbu 'phang mtho /
zhes dang /
ri mthon po gsum de ldong la thob /
ldong zhwa mgo mtho ba de nas byung /
zhes sgrung glu 'di dag gi don ni /
dpe thob kyi glu gnyis dang /
don thob kyi glu gnyis te bzhi /
rus chen bzhir yod pa las /
ldong la dpe thob kyi glu yin te /
ri rtse mo gsum gyi dpe ltar dbu 'phang mtho ba'i don yin zhing /
spyir ldong 'di mang la /
a spo ldong dang lha ldong sogs yod zer /
'di ni phu bo ldong dang /
yum mchog 'bri sga ma zhes bya ba las byung ba'i rigs yin la /
'di la dkar bo ldong dang /
nag po ldong dang /
khra bo ldong dang smug po ldong gi rigs dang bzhi yod la /
'di rigs rnams su 'khrungs pa'i skyes bu dpa' rtsal dgu ldan /
sngon byon dag gi lo rgyus mang /
ldong rigs 'di ni dbus gtsang bar khams a mdo sogs su sngar nas yod /
khyad par du bar khams sa cha 'di ni /
sa yi cha gling gi yul zhes pa ni /
sgang drug las zal mo sgang du grags pa'i sa 'di la /
gling khri gong 'og bar gsum yod pa ni /
gling khri gong ma'i sa ni khams stod 'bri klung gi sa cha rnams dang /
de las b+he sgom gyi rdza ri /
de las phu na g.ya' brag dang /
gangs brag g.ya' bya ba'i ri khrod ngo mtshar can yod pa /

che rgyud dang /
'bring rgyud dang /

blon po ni /

gling dpon mgon thar sku mched da lta bzhugs pa rnams yin zhes /

'bri shing thung can des 'thab na mdzes / /
zhes 'thab 'dzing la bzang ba'i rigs yin zhing /
'bri rje r+wa co can bco brgyad kyi gdung rigs dang /
'bri mi 'gyur thar ba'i gnas brgyad ces /
sa skya dang 'bri gung sogs kyi gdung rigs brgyad dbus gtsang dang bar khams su yod pa dang /
khams kyi gre rong lcags gsum khog dang /

bar khams su lho rong chen bco brgyad kyi nang tshan mgo log zer ba'i sar yang 'bri rigs mang du yod la /
bar skabs shig tu de nas gling gi yul du mi rje bran khol khyim bcu dang bcas te 'ongs nas /
'bri klung gi nyin phyogs 'dzin 'gu kho lung ba zhes bya bar gzhi chags nas ring zhig lon pa'i tshe /
'bri lha rgyal zhes pa'i khyim sngags pa zhig byung /
des gnyan bza' zhig blangs pa'i bu a 'bum rgyal zer ba skyes /
de cher skyes pa'i tshe tsam nas /

lha rgyal /
lha rir mtshams la bzhugs /
bu a 'bum rgyal dpon sar bskos /
gong du bshad pa'i gnyug mar gnas pa'i gnyan mkhar ba gsum gyi mi sde rnams dang tshong 'brel nye shag bsdebs nas 'dug skabs /

phag thar gyi ring la /
rdo khog 'dzi ska rmar khog gsum gyi bdag por gyur /
'di skabs shig la mgo log a 'bum lo go gsum lon dus su 'das /

de la bu bzhi skyes /

kho le sgang thog tu mkhar rdzong gnyis brtsigs /
de'i skabs tA ming rgya rgyal gyis 'jam brid kyi srid jus bstar te grangs nyung mi rigs kyi dpon dag la dpon thob ster ba'i skabs yin pas /
tA ming zon tes phag thar la thang lo ye zhes khri dpon gyi lung byin /
kho rang gi bu bzhi'i gcig ka thog bla ma chos 'bum yin /
che ba rdo rje 'bum la rdo rol gyi sa cha dang mi sde /

rnga khog gi mi sde /
gser khog gi khral /
g.yu dang rtsang khog gi sa cha mi sde rnams thun mong du bzhag ste kho lo gya dgu la 'das /
rdo rje 'bum gyi bu che ba 'bum phyug rgyal dang /
chung ba dbang chen 'bum yin /
padma 'bum gyi bu che ba thar ba dang /
chung ba mgo log dpon po byang chub rgyal mtshan yin /
padma yag gi bu che ba khru 'u dang /
chung ba gnyan thar red /
rdo rje 'bum gyi bu che ba 'bum rgyal gyis smug chen gad 'gor khang ba zhig brtsigs nas bsdad /
bu chung ba dbang chen 'bum pha mkhar du bsdad /
padma 'bum gyi bu che ba thar ba chen mo gdong du pha khyim der bsdad /
chung ba byang chub rgyal mtshan ka thog tu byon /
padma yag gi bu che ba khru 'u gnyan grong gong mar bsdad pas sa der khru 'u nang zer /
chung ba gnyan thar de pha khyim du bsdad par sa der gnyan nang zer /
padma yag gi bu chung ba rtag phan rgyud pa la /
bar skabs su mgo log snying bu mtsho zhes pa byung /
de'i rgyud pa da lta'i mgo log dpal yul tshang yin zer /
'di skabs dbal shul ban zhar gyis mgo log gi dpon rnams la sa zhig bslangs par rdo rje 'bum pha bu nas rdo rol rjes mda' byin /
rdo rje 'bum gyi bu che ba 'bum phyug rgyal la bu gnyis yod pa'i /
che ba mgo log a skyong dang /
dpon mgo log rgyal mtshan nam rin chen 'bum gnyis yin /
padma 'bum gyis 'dzi ska'i stod smad thams cad la dbang bsgyur bas padma 'bum tshang zer ba byung /
padma yag gi sha mdog nag smug yin stabs ban nag zer la /
de'i rgyu mtshan gyis de'i bu khru 'u dang gnyan thar gnyis kyi nang sde thams cad la ban nag tshang zer /

de skabs dbang chen 'bum tshang /
a skyong tshang /
padma 'bum tshang /
padma yag tshang rnams kyis sa bgos nas /
sa mtshams su rdo brtsigs /

bu chung ba tshe mgon yag gi rgyud pa dbang chen stod pa tshang red /
a skyong /
dbang chen 'bum /
padma 'bum 'di gsum la de skabs mgo log khag gsum zer /
a skyong la bu snying bu rgyal dang /
khro bo rgyal gnyis byung ba'i snying bu rgyal ni mi drag rtsal can yin pas /
a skyong gi dbang des bzung zhing /
thang mkhar du da lta'i khang rgan zer ba de brtsigs /
de dang dus mtshungs su padma yag gi bu rgyud mgo log nag ther bu bzhi byung /
snying bu rgyal gyi bu mgo log shAkya 'bum /
des mkhar gong ma brtsigs /
de'i bu tshe dbang 'bum gyis khang ba gsar ba brtsigs pa de la khang gsar zer /

a spo ldong gi rigs kyang yod de /

mkhar ba /
ba le gsum gyi dpon mi sde dang bcas pa'i rgyud pa yod la /
hor gling 'khrug pa'i skabs su yong ba'i dkar bo ldong gi rigs kyang gang sa gang du yod la /

de'i bu /
ge li /
ge tse /
ge 'phan gsum /
ge li dang ge tse'i rgyud pa 'bum skyabs yag dang khro kho sogs yin /
ge 'phan gyi rgyud pa dbal shul ban dpon zer ba'i rgyud du kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa 'khrungs /
de'i rgyud pa tshan gcig lho phyogs kyi g.yu khog rtsang khog sgeg khog rnams bzung bas /
ge 'phan g.yu rtsang sgeg gsum ni /
gser stod dang snyi stod du chags pa de ge 'phan rnying ma dang /
sbra skor ma gnyis ge 'phan stod bza' tshang /
ge tse'i rgyud pa ge tse ma lag thong gsum grags pa rgya che /
zla chu stod sde dge'i mnga' zhabs kyi dpon rigs rnams kyang ge tse'i mi rgyud red /
ge tse dpon po dang ge tse khro shul yang 'di las gyes /
ge rgyal gyi mi'i rgyud pa khams su yod kyang dpon rigs med /
phur ba thar gyi sngon mi rgyud mtsho sngon du mched pa chu yos dus 'khrug dus slar song ba li thang g.yon ru ma dang /
sde gzhung ma zer ba'i dpon rigs /
dbal shul khrom thal ma zer ba'ang yod /
ge li'i bu chung ba ban zhar gyi mi rgyud dbal shul stag skyabs kyis rdo stod rje mang ra'i sa mgo log la bslangs nas der mkhar gzhi bzung /
'di la bu gnyis yod pa'i che ba stag lha 'phan gyi bus /
shos khog tu ru ba byas nas bsdad pa'i rgyud gser thal dpon rigs /
ban zhar nas mi rabs 'ga' song ba'i mtshams khro kho zhes pa'i bu che bas rmar gyi mu nang du 'brog bzung ba'i rgyud pa la mu thal dang /
chung bas khe stod du 'brog bzung ba'i rgyud pa khe thal dpon rigs dbal shul khro kho zer ba 'di yin no / /
dbal shul bu chung gi rgyud pa bu chung rta yag chos gsum 'phan dang bzhi zer ba byung /
a skyabs kyi mi rgyud gser thal ma'i mnga' 'og tu yod /
dbal shul sangs rgyas skyabs kyi bu 'bum skyabs yag de la rdo smad du bu mgon po lhun 'grub dang /
rdo stod du er khe tha'i ji nam mkha' tshe ring /
'dzi ska'i mdar rnam rgyal bkra shis dang gsum /
tha'i ji la dpon 'ju nang gi bdag rkyen che /

sangs rgyas 'bum gyi mi rgyud 'dzi ska'i wa 'bri mgo /
bsu mda' /

da lta 'dzam thang zhes grags pa'i mi ser la ni ldong rigs /
'bri rigs /
sbra rigs sogs rigs du ma zhig yod la de dag ni /
la la bod rgyal btsan po dag gi dus skabs kyi so mtshams srung dmag yin pa dang /
la la ni phyis su 'ongs pa sogs sna tshogs shig yod 'dug bod sil bur thor ba'i rjes su re zhig tsong kha'i rgyal bos dbang bsgyur zhing /
de rjes gling rje ge sar gyis kyang dbang bsgyur /
de rjes gong du bshad pa ltar mgo log gi dpon phag thar gyis rmar shod ma lag drug la dbang bsgyur ba'i gras su 'dzam thang 'dzi ska sogs yod de /
de drug ni gna' mi'i glu gzhas la /
rmar rol ma lag drug gi che ba yin /
rnga khog ba lags skya mo rmar gyi lag rdo khog ri thang phyug mo rmar gyi lag 'dzi ska lha mo dar thang rmar gyi lag g.yu khog stag mo 'phred nyal rmar gyi lag rtsang khog mdo ba kha bkal rmar gyi lag sgeg khog b+han da gru bzhi rmar gyi lag ces zer ba de rnams yin no / /
de rjes phag thar phyi bu 'bum yag padma 'bum 'dzi ska stod smad thams cad kyi sde thams cad dang sa cha'i bdag po byas pas padma 'bum tshang zer ba byung /
padma 'bum gyi bu nag thar gyis chen po gdong mkhar mgo nag mar gser 'bum po ti bcu drug ma bris te /
rab gnas la 'dzam thang chos rje gong ma dang /
ri khrod pa dge ba rgya mtsho zer ba gnyis lhan rgyas gdan drangs te /
'bul chen bzhag 'dzi ska'i myi nag shos mda' man chad dang /
bsi mda' yan chad kyi sa cha dang grwa ba rnams phul /
chos rje gong ma nas 'dzam thang sogs kyi bon 'ga' 'bul dgos gsung ba ltar phul /
de nas chos rje bla ma 'dzam thang phyogs kyi chos srid gnyis ldan du gyur /

rnga khog ni /
rmar rol ma lag drug gi nang tshan yin te /
rnga khog ba lags skya mo rmar gyi lag ces zer ro / /
rmar rol ma lag drug gi sa thams cad la nges tshig yod pa'i nges pa med de /
'dod rgyal gyi ming du ma zhig yod nges la /
rnga ba 'di sa dbyibs kyi sgo nas btags pa yin zer /
sa dbyibs ni rnga 'dra ba'i zlum po zhig yin pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis de ltar btags zer ba /
sa dbyibs la bltas na bden pa 'dra /
'ga' zhig gis sa 'di'i mi rnams mnga' ris nas 'ongs pa yin pas mnga' ba zer ba brda 'gyur ba yin zer ba dang /
chos rgyal 'phags pa'i dus /
dga' ye shes dar rgyas dang ldong shul chen bco brgyad ni mnyam du stod mnga' ris phyogs nas 'ongs pa yin zer ba sogs khungs med kyi gtam du 'khums te mnga' ris pa la mnga' ba dang /
zhang zhung ba la zhang ba dang /
spu rengs pa la spu ba dang /
lha sa ba la lha ba dang /
se ra ba la se ba dang /
'bras spungs pa la 'bras pa dang /
dga' ldan pa la dga' ba zer ba lta bu'i bdag sgra can gyi tshig sdud ni sngar ma mthong zhing bod kyi mkhas pa dag gis ma mdzad la /
de lta bu'i tshig sdud ni /
rig pa'i gzhung lugs dang /

ldong shul chen bco brgyad ni /
a spo ldong gi rigs las gyes pa mdo khams stod smad kun tu sngar nas yod pa rus mdzod dag tu gsal zhing /
dga' ye shes dar rgyas ni khri ral gyi dus su khral bsdu ru mdo smad 'dir 'ongs pas bstan pa snga dar gyi dus yin pa dang /
chos rgyal 'phags pa bstan pa phyi dar gyi skabs yin pas /
de'i dus su dga' ye shes dar rgyas gsar du slebs pa min pas /
bshad tshul de dag ni rtog bzo 'ba' zhig go / /
des na sa 'dir sa gzhan dang 'dra bar gna' dus nas bod rigs yod nges /

thang dmag gis gzhi bzung ste /

smad ba le'i sa yin /

de nas dme thas chung don 'grub /
'di 'phror cog tse'i tsha bu myi glen zhig de'i chung mar bsus pa yin nam zer ba'i dme rgyal mo a 'bos bza' zhes pas dbang yun ring bzung /
de'i 'phror a skyong bde sgron dang blon po dme dkon gnyis kas dbang bzung /
de'i 'phror dbal shul rdo smad nas dbal shul lcags thar 'bum zer ba dme tshang gi bu skal du blangs nas /

bdag mo skra dkar ma zer /
de gnyis kyi bu mgon po bsod nams /
des a skyong gong ma'i bu mo zhig blangs mod /
ma 'grig par skal ba byin nas phud /

bu mo'i ming la dpal chen don 'grub mtsho /

bu mo don 'grub mtsho gnyis skyes /

zhing skyong pha bu'i ring la /

rnga stod kyi dpon 'ga' re dbang du mi 'du ba re gnyis bsad zer /
rgya stod rdor zhar dang ma 'grig de skabs dme rgyal bo dang yang ma mthun pas /
dme dmag yab kyi steng du rgyug rgyu gra sgrig byed skabs /
yab kyis tshor nas mtshan mor bros byol byas /
de'i don du bla brang gi dmag chen bud pa khang gsar tshang sogs dpon po 'gas bar chings byas te dmag rdzogs byin nas dmag phyir slog de rjes 'jam dbyangs bzhad sprul rin po che dbus phyogs su phebs skabs /
lam bar nas khang gsar paN chen dang /
a mchog 'on po gnyis gzu ba byas te gyod bshad /
de skabs bla brang phyag mdzod mkhyen rab don 'grub zer bas dbang 'dzin pa'i skabs yin la khong gyod sna kha mchur thugs mi dgyes pa zhig yin gshis gyod 'grig thabs byas zer /
yab kyi gson stong la dngul rdo tshad sum brgya 'jal rgyu byas te gyod legs par 'grig 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i mchog sprul rin po ches dme blon 'khor bcas la tshe dbang gnang nas /
dme tshang gis chos 'brel bzhag de rjes bla brang phyag mdzod rjes ma dbal mang tshang dang dme rgyal dpal mgon 'phrin las gnyis mna' mthun byas te /

!!rnga ba'i dme dpon mos gdan drangs te /

!!'di dus dme'i dpon rgyud rdzogs nas /

de nas rgyal khang du khong gi dbu zhwa dang /

de dag ji ltar yin gyi gsung gsal dang /

de dus 'dzam gling du skad grags che ba'i dmag 'khrug byas pa'i sa cha /
zung chu ? zhes pa'i chu bo'i mjug dang nye ba'i ri sgang la sa rdo 'dres pa'i gyang brdungs pa'i 'thab rdzong mthon po mang bo yod pa deng sang da dung ma zhig par yod /
de dus su mtha' mtshams srung ba'i dmag mi gtan sdod byas pa'i bod mi ni /

chos 'dul ba'i kun spyod gtsang zhing 'chad nyan 'phel ba'i dgon sde grags pa can zhig yin /
deng sang gi sa khra'i thog tu /
a mgon ru la a dgan ro zhes dang /
a rngang ru la /
a sngon ro zhes dang /
mgo ba ro zhes pa'i gtan med kyi sde ba zhig bsnan pa sogs /
dngos tshul dang mi mthun pa'i gtam mi nyung ba re bris 'dug yul der ming thogs tshul bshad na /
dmu dge zhes pa'i ming thogs tshul gong du bshad zin pa ltar yin /
stod tsho dgu'i nang tshan nor ba ru ni /
'og gi zhing ba rnams kyi phyugs rigs 'tsho skyong du rtswa chu bzang sa der 'ongs nas bsdad pa phyis su gzhis chags pa la nor ba ru zhes ming chags /
nor zhes pa phyugs rigs kyi spyi ming du 'bod pa'i stabs kyis /
phyugs rigs 'tsho mkhan la nor ba /
zhes 'bod pa'i goms 'dris byung /
de'i 'og gi sde ba sog po ru /
zhes pa sngar sog po'i phyogs nas mi bdun sprang 'khyams lta bur byas nas 'ongs te /
sa der thog mar 'dug sa'i sa de la /
sprang bo'i gad thog zer /
de nas sa der zhing las byas te dar zhing rgyas nas sog po ru zer ba'i mi sde 'di chags /
de'i 'og gi sngar sa stong skabs wa mo'i tshang yod sa de la zhing las byas te gzhi chags pa la wa tshang ru zer /
de'i 'og tu sngar sa stong skabs shing sdong sogs su bya'i tshang mang bo yod pa'i sa der yang sngar bzhin gzhi chags pa'i sde ba la bya tshang ru zer /
de'i 'og tu gzhi chags pa'i sde ba khe tshong ru zhes pa ni /
thog mar khe tshong byas nas phyug por gyur pa'i khyim tshang zhig gis gzhi bzung bas /
khe tshong ru zhes thogs /
nor ba ma brtsis pa'i gong gi sde ba bzhi la stod tsho bzhi zer /
de'i 'og gi sde ba la sngar bla grwa du ma yod pas chos dang dge ba la 'bad pas /
chos ru zhes thogs /
de'i 'og tu a mgon zer ba'i mi zhig gis gzhi bzung bas /
a mgon ru zhes thogs /

a chu lung ba'i chu'i ming la brten nas /
a chu ru zer /
'di la rgya mi bu mo spun gsum gyis gzhi bzung bas a lce zer zhes sa khra'i thog tu bris pa khungs med pa'i rdzun gtam red /
a chu lung ba de la deng sang shing ra zer zhing /
lung ba'i kha stod la shing ra'i kha zer /
gong gi sde ba de bzhi la cha rngang tsho bzhi zer zhing /
sde ba 'di bzhi dang stod tsho bzhi nor ba dang bcas pa'i sde ba 'di dgu la stod tsho dgu zer /
zhing khong gi chu dang /
dmu dge'i chu 'dres mtshams kyi ri sngo ljang gi ther khug tu zhing btab nas gzhi chags pa'i sde ba la sngo ther ru /
sngo ther dang de'i stod kyi 'brong tsha zer ba'i sa cha gnyis kyi bar du zhing sa gshin po yod sar gzhi chags pa'i sde ba la bar zhing ru zer /
zhing khong chu'i byang gi lung lag cig gi nang du /
thog mar shes rab zer ba'i mi zhig gis gzhi bzung ste rim gyis sde bar chags pa la shes rab ru zer /
sa de'i g.yon phyogs kyi ltem thog cig la /
thog mar a gsa' zhes bya ba'i mi zhig gis gzhi bzung nas rim gyis sde bar chags pa la /
a gsa' ru zer /
sde ba de bzhi la chu chung tsho bzhi zer /
rgyam kho zer ba'i mi zhig gis gzhi bzung sde chags pa'i sde ba la rgyam kho ru zer /
de'i 'og tu dge yag ces pa'i mi zhig gis gzhi bzung nas chags pa'i sde ba la /
dge yag ru zer /
de'i 'og tu brag ri'i gshong yod sar chags pa'i sde ba la brag gshong ru zer /
de'i 'og gi sde ba la smad pa ru zer /
sde ba de bzhi la smad tsho bzhi zer /
de'i 'og tu bla ro ru zer ba yod la /

mdo smad 'di blon po mgar gyi bu bzhis bzung /
bu che ba blon chen dang /
gzhan gsum dmag dpon red /
de dus 'di phyogs kyi bod blon gyis gzhi bzung ba'i mkhar gtso bo la /
'phan kru'u ? zer la /
de yod sa ni /
deng dus kyi chos rje dgon pa'i gong gi 'a zha zhes pa'i sa de yin pas /
mkhar shul yang da dung yod zer /
de skabs su mdo smad phyogs 'dir /
'a zha dang /
sum pa dang /
gru gu dang /
mi nyag sogs yod mod /
sum pa ni gnya' khri btsan pos bod gong bu gcig gyur byed pa'i skabs su /
dbang du bsdu bya'i bod kyi rgyal phran bcu gnyis kyi grangs su yod pas bod yin /
'a zha yang /
rus mdzod las /
"ldong la rus chen bco brgyad grol /
seng rgyal 'a zha bu dgu grol /
" zhes gsungs pa ltar 'a zha yang bod yin mod /
bod kyi rgyal phran 'di tsho skabs 'gar /
btsan po'i mnga' 'og tu mi sgur bas dmag song nas 'dul dgos byung ba red /
gru gu ni bod yin par mi snang yang bod kyis btsan 'dul byas te /
bod rigs su thim par nges /
mi nyag ni /
sngon bod rgyal la spun gsum yod pa'i gcig ni bod kyi rgyal bo dang /
gcig ni 'brug pa'i ? rgyal bo dang /
gcig ni bzhin nag po can zhig yin pa mnga' ris dang bcas pa logs su bsdad pa la mi nag zer ba /
phyis su brda 'gyur nas mi nyag ? ces grags mod rtsa ba bod yin no / /
hor rgyal rabs ? kyi skabs su /
hor rgyal gyis bod chol kha gsum sa skya ba la dbang yon du phul stabs /
sa skyas bskos pa'i bod dpon 'dug sa ni zung chu'i a stong gi sa cha yin la /
a stong dgon pa'i gong du /
bang hrang mkhar zhes pa'i mkhar shul yod la /
de dang nye bar gling ba sang zhes pa'i khyim tshang yod sa de /
de dus kyi btson khang gi shul yin pas /
khang ba bskyar bzo byed skabs khang ba'i sa 'og nas /
btson chas 'ga' zhig bud zer /
gang ltar hor gyi skabs su sa skya bas dbang bsgyur bas sngar bzhin bod kyis bzung /
zung chu'i sa 'di yang thang the tsung dus nas lo bdun brgya bzhi bcu'i bar bod rkyang bas bzung mod /
tA ming rgyal bo ? hung u ? dus su rim gyis bod kyi sa cha wun khron dang we kru'u /
mung kru'u sogs la rgya dmag slebs te 'khrug rtsod byed bzhin zung chur slebs /
sngar gyi sung kru'u dang /
'phan kru'u gnyis gcig sdud byas te zung chu'i chu thog tu mkhar brtsigs /
cin the'i ? skabs su mkhar nang du lha khang bzhengs te dgon pa byas /
lcags phag lo'i gsar brje'i bar du /
bod mi ser dmag gis zung chu'i mkhar lan gsum bsregs pa'i lo rgyus snang /
bcings 'grol byas rjes mkhar 'dir bde 'jags ngang 'dzugs skrun byed bzhin la /
lhag par da skabs dar zhing rgyas bzhin yod do / /
mdzod dge'i sa 'di mdo smad sa gzhan dag ltar /
gna' snga mor bod chags pa'i sa yul yin mod /
sngar bshad pa ltar thang gi rgyal bo dar ba'i skabs /
yul 'di dag thang gis bzung ste /
kru'u mang bo btsugs /
de rjes srong btsan sogs bod kyi btsan po stobs ldan dag gi dus su /
rgya mi mtha' skrod byas rjes sa 'di sa stong du gyur /
mnga' bdag khri ral ba can gyi dus su /
ka ci'i mchod rten dkar bo yan chod bod kyi mnga' 'og yin stabs /
dga' ye shes dar rgyas zer ba'i bod blon zhig khral bsdu ru 'ongs /
des sa 'dir chu bo chen po gsum 'bab cing /
rtswa chu shin tu bzang bas /
sa stong du bskyur mi bra /
sa 'dir 'brog sde 'dzugs dgos zer nas sa 'dir gzhi bzung /
de'i bu rgyud che ba dga' stag thul can dang /
chung ba dga' spyang thul can gnyis yin /
dga' stag ris can nam dga' stag thul can gyi bu rgyud la bla ma dge 'dun zer ba byung /
de dpon dang rgya nag tu 'gro ba'i bla ma chen po dag gi phyag mdzod byas /
'gro 'ong mang du byas pas /
phyag mdzod dge 'dun nam /
mdzod pa dge 'dun zhes ming can zhig byung /
de'i mi rgyud ru sde bcas la mdzod dge zhes pa'i ming thogs /
spyang thul can gyi mi rgyud ni mdzod dge smad dam /
mdzod dge dme bo zer ba de dang /
co ne'i dpon rgyud rnams yin /
rigs 'di la dga' rigs zer ba'i rgyu mtshan ni /
sngon bod kyi rgyal rigs rgyal sa ma thob pa zhig la bu med nas /
thang lha sogs yul lha rnams la gsol ba btab pas /
nam mkhar 'ja' tshon dang bcas te bu zhig byung bas shin tu dga' bar gyur /
de'i rigs la dga' rigs zer /
rus chen bzhi'i nang gi sga rigs dang mig cig ces rus mdzod las bshad /
mdzod dge 'dir bod kyi 'brog sde chags nas yun ring 'gor rjes /
rab byung ma tshugs gong gi drug cu skor de'i nang gling seng chen byung nas /
hor gling 'khrug pa'i skabs /
thog mar hor 'di phyogs su slebs nas sa mang bo bzung mod /
gling gis hor dmag pham par byas te rma stod smad bar gsum gling gi mnga' 'og tu gyur /
gling gi srid nyams rjes sde shog so sor gyes /
rim gyis mdzod dge shog bcu gnyis su gyur /
mdzod dge shog bcu gnyis ni /

'breng ba /

gza' ru rnams so / /
snga ma brgyad ni 'brog sde dang /
phyi ma bzhi ni rong sde red /
thang skor ni byams me las chad pa dang /
sog tshang ni sog tshang bla ma'i su hrug pa 'phel ba dang /
nang ba ni chos rje bla ma'i su hrug pa 'phel ba yin zer /
dga' ye shes dar rgyas kyi rgyud pa rnams mdzod dge'i dpon khag so sor gyes tshul las /
stod ma'i dpon po'i rgyud pa ni /
mdzod dge'i dpon sngon mas reb bza' /
stag ring bza' /
'bal bza' gsum blangs pa'i mnga' ma gsum ga la bu gsum skyes /
mna' ma che ba reb bza'i bus rme stod bzung ba'i rgyud pa deng sang gi mdzod dge stod mar grags pa red gsungs /
mna' ma 'bring ba stag ring bza'i bus rma rme ska gsum gyi bar nas sa bzung ba'i rgyud pa mdzod dge byams me dang /
mtshams shig thang bza' zhig blangs pa'i rgyud pa la thang skor thogs /
'di'i dpon bkra shis dbang dang sog tshang dpon pos ska rma 'dres mtshams su ri khrod btab pa da lta'i sog tshang dgon red /
ska chu ska bar stag rtse nas 'bab pa'i stod du a mchog smra dpon gyis sbyin bdag byas te /
'bras spungs sgo mang gi 'bul sdud pa 'phan po sman pa ngag dbang sbyin pas byams me'i dgon pa btab /
'debs mkhan gyi dbang gis 'bras spungs dgon du grags /
mnga' ma chung ba 'bal bza'i bu blo gros bzang /
de'i bu rgyud 'bos dpon po /
gling ba'i dpon po /
bzhag ldom dpon po /
mdzod dge smad kyi shog kha lnga'i dpon rnams kyang blo gros bzang gi mi rgyud red zer /
'bos dpon po 'bal bza' bu rgyud kyi pha khyim yin pas 'bal zur chag zer /
gling dpon rab brtan gyi bu a 'brug gis rma rme 'dres mtshams su sa bzung /
lo brgyad bcu lhag la bsdad kyang dgra rkun dang gyod zer ba rna bas thos ma myong bar grags /
'di la bu bdun yod pa'i rgyud pa so sor gyes /
bu che 'og lcags rgyal gyi sde khrod du the bo bum pa'i ru ba mang bas bum skor zer /
'bring bo a snying la'ang rgyud pas yod /
'bring 'og a klum pha khyim du bsdad /
des mda' dmar gzhung gi sa bzung ba'i rgyud pa la phyi ra stod smad bar gsum du grags /
hu ra stod smad bar gsum yang 'di'i rgyud pa red zer /
a klum gyi bu chung ba'i rgyud pa bla ma tshul khrims rin chen gyis gling ba'i r+wa bong dgon btab /
mdzod dge a 'brug gi chun ma ho bza' la bu gsum yod pa'i rgyud par ho bza'i bu rgyud zer /
bzhag ldom ni bzhag ldom gyi mes po gong ma zhig gis gling ba dang dme byas /
pha yul dme rkyen du bzhag ste ldom nas song bas 'gro mkhan mdzod dge dme bo yin de ltar thogs zer /
bong tshang gi rgyud pa bong tshang bla ma zer bas /
de phyogs kyi rnying ma bsgyur te gsar ma byas so / /

chu dkar gyi stod du /

dwags po zer zhing /

de dag gi goms 'dris chos lugs sogs kyang bod spyi dang 'dra'o / /

mi ser dag la ni rus sna tshogs shig yod par mngon /

tsha ru /
